In addition to hiring lawyer Li Hongyu as legal counsel, the Labor Union issued a circular saying that Cao Jianting harbored traitors, falsely accused fellow workers, arbitrarily arrested committee members, did not accept party and government mediation, incited labor unrest, disrupted the labor movement, and obstructed the national salvation movement, and requested that he be immediately removed and punished, otherwise, the bureau would be responsible for any incidents that occurred. (Special Telegram, 31st)

(Special Telegram, 31st)

Ministry of Railways Orders Two Railways to Start Restoring the Mongolia-Tea Joint Transportation

(Nanjing) In the past, the Mongolia-Tea was transported via a joint transportation on PingSui and PingHan railways since the 10th year of the Republic and the export was not small. Later it was stopped without proper procedures after the severance of relations between China and Russia. In the current atmosphere of resuming relations, the said joint transportation should be restored to increase the railways income. Thus the Department ordered PingSui and PingHan Railways to convene and prepare and also ordered PingHan to investigate the transport situation of Tea in Hankou and negotiate the responsibility for the joint transportation with PingSui Railways. (Special Telegram, 31st)

Current Affairs Commentary

The Murkiness of the Quadrangle Relationship Between China, America, Britain, and Japan

(1) The Friendly Future of Sino-American Relations

Since the Democratic and Republican parties competed in the United States last June, their platforms have largely leaned towards domestic issues. Regarding diplomatic relations, the Democratic Party has not made any concrete expressions. Regarding the Far East issue, it is particularly vague. As a result, general speculation at the time was that if Roosevelt were elected, the United States' foreign policy towards the Far East would undergo fundamental changes. However, based on past history, we know that there is no fundamental difference between the Democratic Party's foreign policy and the Hoover-Stimson Doctrine. Let us cite the fact that in 1915, when Japan forced China to accept the Twenty-One Demands, Democratic President Wilson was in office. In his note to Japan on May 13 of the same year, he stated:

"The United States cannot recognize any agreement concluded between China and Japan that would harm China's territorial and political integrity or the international policy of the Open Door."

Seventeen years have passed, and this has not changed. When the Republican Party was in power, it focused its efforts on resolving European war debts. However, European countries are already exhausted. Apart from exploiting colonies and semi-colonies to replenish their resources, it is difficult to find a way to regenerate themselves. Even if the United States can control Europe, it will not develop much. It will only be able to temporarily maintain the status quo. Therefore, since President Roosevelt XXVI, it has been recognized that the center of gravity of the world will shift to the Pacific. After the economic panic of 1929, the situation in Europe deteriorated daily, and the current situation in the Americas was difficult to maintain. Although there have been repeated estimates that the panic has reached its lowest point and that a turnaround will be seen in the future, facts have proven them to be wrong. However, the economic situation in the Far East, even though China is externally invaded by strong enemies and internally ravaged by bandits, with people having nowhere to escape death, rural areas becoming increasingly bankrupt, and cities gradually declining, the people's energy to endure hardship and the abundance of natural resources are still enough to shock the world and may transform the current difficult situation. Therefore, even under such a fragmented situation, the United States' exports to China in 1932 were still over 260 million taels. Although the amount in gold dollars is less than 100 million US dollars, it actually ranks first in imports to China. No one can deny the hope for the future. The close relationship between China and the United States, based on trade alone, is worthy of extra attention. However, the reason for the decrease in import and export trade in 1932 compared to 1931 was that the Japanese army illegally occupied the three northeastern provinces and bombarded Shanghai, destroying Zhabei and Wusong, causing China to suffer a huge impact. General purchasing power has therefore declined. Although we lack accurate and precise statistics, we can estimate that it has decreased by one-third to one-half compared to the past. This loss is directly felt by our country, but is it not indirectly damaging to our friendly neighbors as well? The Japanese military aggression is to blame. It is the Japanese imperialists who are destroying peace in the Pacific. The United States cannot tolerate this for long, whether from a political or economic standpoint. At a minimum, it must adhere to its "non-recognition (of gains by force) doctrine." Therefore, President Roosevelt has unofficially stated that he will not change the Hoover-Stimson Far East policy after taking office. After seeing justice trampled by iron hooves, we believe that this move by the United States is a glimmer of hope for the future of peace and is the foundation for friendly relations between China and the United States.

(2) Deterioration of US-Japan Relations

Our country has fully recognized the poison of Japanese military aggression. Its barbarity cannot be reasoned with. We have appealed to the League of Nations, hoping to extend our grievances and maintain peace and justice together. However, due to our weak strength and the lack of determination of the authorities to respond to violence with iron and blood, Japan has been able to indulge its greed. If the previous situation continues, and our country continues to follow the unwise policy of "verbal resistance and actual concession," then Japan will intensify its encroachment strategy. First, take Rehe and eastern Hebei, then Hebei and Shandong. In three to five years, if it can use force to overcome the current economic difficulties and successfully exploit the three northeastern provinces as a resource, then it will be easy to extend from the Yangtze River basin to the Philippines and other islands in Southeast Asia, realizing its dream of an East Asian Monroe Doctrine.

The United States believes that since the September 18th Incident, the Japanese national economic crisis has gradually unfolded. Its rural debt was 4 billion yen in 1930, 4.7 billion yen in 1931, and by the end of last year, the total has exceeded 9 billion yen. As for the national debt, it has also increased over time. By January 1933, it had reached 7 billion. Adding the 1 billion yen in public debt to cover the budget shortfall this year and the loss on foreign debt due to exchange rates, the actual total national debt should be over 9 billion yen. The cost of invading the three northeastern provinces alone has been 400 million yen in the past year and four months. This year, it will cost at least 200 million. If this continues, the weak Japanese people will not be able to bear it. Therefore, for its own sake and for the sake of controlling hegemony in the Pacific, the United States seems to think that waiting for Japan to collapse on its own is the best policy. However, this assumption is only a one-dimensional observation. If the three northeastern provinces are relatively stable, they can be easily obtained. At least, they can thereby plunder military resources for future use in the Pacific War.

Moreover, there has long been a clear understanding between Britain and Japan. This is evidenced by Simon's pro-Japanese remarks and the recent rumors of guaranteeing that "the League of Nations will never invoke Article 16 of the Covenant" and opposing the statement in the report that the puppet organization will not be recognized. From this point forward, Japan can boldly invade China, with Britain providing assistance from behind. This will not only help Japan invade China but will also help Japan against the United States, to the point of undermining the balance of power in the Far East and trampling on world peace. Can this situation be resolved by waiting? I am afraid that the longer we wait, the more irreparable the damage in the Far East will be.

The relationship between the United States and Japan is such, and Britain's attitude is also like this. The United States still has two oceans as a boundary and can barely protect itself. However, it seems unable to escape the control of Japanese imperialism over eastern markets. Even if our country can get the sympathy of the United States at this time, it will only be limited to spiritual assistance. Then, in the actual national struggle, is there any other way but for our people to fight with iron and blood and work hard to save themselves?

The United States Navy's Elite Pacific Grand Maneuvers

~The Greatest Test of Defensive Capabilities~

~Scheduled Duration: Seventy Days~

According to the Tokyo Nichinichi Shimbun, the joint naval exercises of the United States' Pacific and Atlantic Fleets commenced on January 23rd. The Atlantic reconnaissance fleet, under the command of Admiral Cluverius, departed from its three bases: San Diego, San Pedro, and Mayport, on the 23rd, heading towards the attacking force's base in Honolulu. This grand maneuver, centered on Honolulu and the American Pacific coast, is what the U.S. Navy Department calls "the greatest test of the defensive capabilities of the American West Coast." It involves 167 naval vessels, 250 aircraft, and the airship Akron. The plan is to launch a vigorous attack on Ford Island in Honolulu, which is hypothetically occupied by the enemy. The scheduled duration is 70 days, during which a major naval battle will be fought on the seas around Honolulu and the American Pacific coast. As for the Pacific attacking force, it is mainly composed of the Atlantic Fleet, organized as the "Black Fleet," aiming to occupy a part of the Pacific coast. On the 23rd, seven cruisers and the aircraft carrier USS Lexington were dispatched from San Pedro naval port, and the aircraft carrier USS Saratoga and twelve destroyers were sent from the two bases of San Diego and Mayport, heading towards Honolulu. These three fleets will converge at sea and arrive in Honolulu on January 31st to form the Black Fleet. It is planned that on February 6th, an operation will be launched to seize San Pedro and San Diego on the American West Coast. Simultaneously, the "Blue Fleet" will defend the West Coast, preventing the Black Fleet's actions and launching a counterattack, striving to completely annihilate the Black Fleet. Submarines, aircraft, and modern weapons will be used to scout the Black Fleet's movements. It is also reported that the commander of the U.S. Joint Fleet is Admiral Leigh. Leigh has ordered a new cruiser squadron to be permanently stationed in San Pedro. This squadron is composed of seven six-inch gun cruisers from the Atlantic Fleet and is part of the Pacific Battle Fleet, in order to increase the fighting power of the Pacific Fleet.

A Reuters dispatch from Honolulu on the 30th stated that the joint military exercises of the U.S. Army and Navy officially began today. Part of it is a simulated attack on Honolulu, so the defending forces on Oahu Island are making full preparations today. All gun muzzles within the fortified areas have been turned towards the sea in preparation for the attacking forces' assault in the next two days. On Friday, 10,000 defending troops were dispatched from their camps and deployed in strategic locations. Their artillery positions are all camouflaged, and even at a short distance, their locations are unknown. The latest high-altitude anti-aircraft guns have also been placed at various key points, reportedly having very strong firepower, capable of preventing enemy aircraft from flying low and losing their bomb-hitting effectiveness. The preparations for this exercise are widely believed to indicate whether an enemy fleet approaching the American Pacific coast can destroy America's strongly defended position in the Pacific. This year's exercise in the Honolulu area is quite short but can be considered important. American military experts are confident that any enemy attacking the American West Coast will not leave the Pearl Harbor base behind undefended, as American forces can launch an effective counter-offensive from Pearl Harbor against the enemy's very long lines of communication.

Economic Conflict Between Japan and Great Britain

After the September 18th Incident, the boycott of Japanese goods was very strong in our country. Therefore, Japanese goods, on the one hand, followed the army deep into various parts of the three northeastern provinces, and military supplies were shipped to the Northeast in huge quantities. In Japan's foreign trade in 1932, the three northeastern provinces actually increased by 3%. The status in the past three years is as follows:

%

1930 5.9

1931 5.7

1932 8.9

The reason for the decrease in Japanese goods in the three northeastern provinces in 1931 compared to 1930 was due to the boycott caused by the Wanpaoshan Incident. After the invasion in 1931, Japanese goods have been advancing directly with guns, even to this day. In our own country, Japanese goods have been decreasing year by year, and the actual situation is as follows:

%

1930 21.5

1931 16.8

1932 12.2

It can be seen that in these three years, there has been a decrease of 9.3%, that is, Japanese goods in China have decreased by 10% of the total exports. In the process of the Sino-Japanese conflict, Japanese goods have advanced into British colonies. In British Malaya, India, and Australia, they compete with British products. Last year, cotton and silk fabrics increased by about 80 million yuan, mostly in India and the above-mentioned areas, competing fiercely with Lancashire products. British products were completely defeated. In order to win in the commercial war, Britain held the Ottawa Conference to study countermeasures to prevent Japanese goods. The status of trade with Britain is listed below:

British Mainland British Colonies Total

% % %

1930 4.1 18.5 22.6

1931 4.7 20.2 24.9

1932 4.2 27.0 31.2

It can be seen that in British-Japanese trade, there has not been much change in the British mainland in these three years. However, in British colonies, the quantity of Japanese goods imported has increased by 8.5% of Japan's gold exports. It can be said that what was lost in China was gained in Britain. Therefore, the capital war between Britain and Japan has become even more fierce. During this period, the relationship between China, the United States, and Japan gradually weakened. The changes are as follows:

%

1930 36.8

1931 39.4

1932 33.4

There was a decrease of 3.4% in three years. Comparing 1932 with 1931, there was a decrease of 6%. Japanese goods have gradually lost their sales in China and the United States. Although Japanese goods are promoted in various parts of the three northeastern provinces with guns, judging from the overall situation, what is gained cannot compensate for what is lost. By looking at the import of Japanese goods in the whole of China, one can understand this reason:

%

1930 27.4

1931 22.5

1932 21.1

Judging from the standpoint of the commercial war, the competition between Britain and Japan is very fierce. Britain cannot be Japan's good friend forever. In the Malay Peninsula, in order to promote Japanese goods, Japanese merchants enter the villages and collude with the locals, leading them to organize cooperatives to sell all Japanese goods. The Japanese side provides various conveniences, and political connections are established through economic relations. Therefore, the British are very wary of the Japanese. From the perspective that the commercial war gradually leads to a political war between Britain and Japan, although Britain is currently very helpful to Japan politically, this kind of atmosphere is gradually brewing inside. It can be concluded that Britain and Japan cannot be good friends forever.

Formation of the New French Cabinet

Premier Daladier Concurrently Heads the Army, Paul-Boncour Remains as Foreign Minister

Socialist Party Refuses to Cooperate with the New Government

Havas, Paris, January 31st. Former Minister of the Army Daladier has now formed a new cabinet. The list of cabinet members is as follows:

Premier Daladier, concurrently Minister of the Army; Minister of Justice and Deputy Premier Béranger; Paul-Boncour, Minister of Foreign Affairs; Chautemps, Minister of the Interior; Chéron, Minister of Finance; Lamoureux, Minister of Budget; Leygues (reappointed), Minister of the Navy; de Chappedelaine, Minister of Merchant Marine; it seems that the former Minister of Aviation of the previous cabinet, Painlevé, did not agree to take the original position due to health reasons.

Reuters, Paris, January 31st. This morning, the Chamber of Deputies passed 4,000,000,000 francs for the political expenses of February, and the Senate will also pass it this afternoon. Thus, the new government has the political expenses for January and can calmly propose the budget案. The new cabinet is scheduled to appear in Congress on February 3rd.

Reuters, Paris, January 30th. Daladier had asked the Socialist Party to join the new cabinet. The Socialist Party replied this afternoon. The Socialist Party voted 64 to 17 to conditionally accept the Premier's invitation. The conditions attached were that Daladier must be guided by the principles of a special environment and the political program passed by the Socialist Party last June. The Socialist Party's political program includes: 1) Actively reducing military spending; 2) Nationalizing the insurance industry; 3) Prohibiting the arms trade; 4) Balancing the budget, but not reducing the funding for social undertakings, official salaries, or pensions.

Reuters, Paris, January 31st. Daladier has not yet been able to obtain the support of the Socialist Party because the Socialist Party's conditions are extreme and cannot be accepted by Daladier. However, Daladier is not discouraged by this failure and has still formed a purely Radical Party cabinet.

The Hitler Cabinet Announces its Policy Program

=Strictly Abiding by the Scope of the Constitution=

=Absolutely No Oppression of the Communist Party=

The National Assembly Will Be Convened in Early February

Havas, Berlin, January 30th. The new cabinet held its first meeting this afternoon, chaired by Premier Hitler. Hitler stated that today is of great significance as it marks the unification of national forces to form a new cabinet. The new Premier then explained the general principles of his policy program and his attitude towards the National Assembly, which was unanimously approved by all cabinet members.

Havas, Berlin, January 30th. The new Minister of the Interior, Frick, issued a declaration to the press, stating that the new government's policy program is: 1) to advocate freedom of speech; 2) to absolutely not prohibit the Communist Party; 3) to resolutely not continue the constitutional reform plan of the Papen cabinet; 4) to resolutely not declare a state of national emergency.

Havas, Berlin, January 30th. The new Premier Hitler issued a proclamation to the Nazi Party, declaring that nationalist parties and organizations have now united to fight together for the restoration of Germany. He also stated that the Nazis have succeeded in the enormous responsibilities they have shouldered. In conclusion, he asked party members to trust him so that he has the power to rebuild Germany on the basis of honor, freedom, and social peace.

National Society, Berlin, January 31st. It is now believed that after the establishment of the new mixed government in Germany, there will be some financial and political reforms. However, according to Hitler's spokesman, there will be no drastic changes that would cause unrest, and Hitler will govern the country according to law and reason. It is reported that all cabinet members except the Minister of Justice were decided before the announcement of Hitler's cabinet formation. However, the position of Minister of Justice is still vacant and will be filled after the Center Party decides whether to participate. The Standing Committee of the National Assembly held a meeting today and decided to convene the National Assembly no later than February 7th. The new government will announce its major policies to the National Assembly on this day. It has been announced today that the representative to the Disarmament Conference will be personally assumed by the Chief of Defense, General Blomberg.

Maintaining Fiscal Credit Externally

Considering Unemployment Relief Internally

Havas, Berlin, 30th - The new Director of the Federal Government Information Bureau, Mr. Funk, met with foreign journalists tonight and made a statement saying that any attempts at monetary and economic experiments that would hinder political standing will not be undertaken by the new government. He also stated, "We are willing to live in peace with everyone; this is the basis of our policy."

National, Berlin, 31st - The new cabinet discussed some new plans at a cabinet meeting this morning. It is said that the main focus of consideration was an unemployment relief plan, including the adoption of forced labor after raising considerable funds. Rumors have spread that the President of the Deutsche Bank, Luther, will soon resign and be replaced by the former President, Schacht. The authorities have declared that this news is unfounded from the government's point of view. The new cabinet has absolutely no intention of experimenting with finance or fiscal policy.

The Center Party Adopts a Wait-and-See Attitude

Havas, Berlin, 31st - The new Chancellor Hitler conferred with the leader of the Center Party, Cardinal Kaas, this morning, hoping to at least gain the Center Party's tolerance of the government. According to the Center Party's newspaper, the "Germania," the party is not making things difficult for the government at present but is waiting for the government's administrative program before making a decision. Therefore, the Center Party may temporarily adopt a wait-and-see attitude and temporarily tolerate the Hitler-Papen coalition cabinet. Therefore, when a vote of no confidence in the government is proposed in the House of Representatives, the party will not participate in the vote. Some in the National Socialist Party advocate immediately dissolving the House of Representatives to hold new elections, as Hitler's rise to power has made a deep impression on the public, which may allow the party to attract some new voters. However, the government does not think so, believing that even if the House of Representatives does not trust the government, there is no need to hold a re-election, because after the House of Representatives is dissolved, the government can postpone the new election indefinitely.

National Socialist Party Members Celebrate Fiercely

Havas, Berlin, 30th - National Socialist Party members celebrated Hitler's assumption of the chancellorship fiercely. The Stahlhelm also scheduled a torchlight procession in front of the State Council tonight. Starting at 6:00 PM, the National Socialist Party held a celebration. Thousands of people stood and watched at several places in the central district of Berlin, including Wilhelmstrasse, Brandenburg Gate, the Victory Column, and Unter den Linden. At 8:00 PM, 15,000 National Socialist Party members marched in orderly steps past the State Council. Hitler stood on the balcony, looking down from above. The public cheered loudly at Hitler from the streets. In the evening, Communist Party members held demonstrations in many places to oppose the Hitler cabinet, but they were dispersed by the police, and several people were arrested.

Communist Party Sabotage Plan Fails

National, Berlin, 31st - The Communist Party's plan to incite a general strike across the country this morning has failed everywhere. Only in Hamburg did radical shop assistants announce a general strike, but it was also unsuccessful. The party's main newspaper, "Die Rote Fahne," was ordered to be suspended indefinitely by the authorities because it published an article this morning calling on the people to stage a political general strike. Today, the people of the country are working as usual.

National, 31st, Berlin - Apart from minor clashes between the Communist Party and the National Socialist Party in Berlin, Halle, and Düsseldorf at night, it was relatively quiet. The most serious incident in Berlin was when a squad of the National Socialist Party's Sturmabteilung (SA) was fired upon while passing through an area inhabited by Communist Party members. One policeman and one SA member were killed. When the SA returned fire, several Communist Party members were seriously injured. The working-class areas of the capital were almost deserted, apparently because workers were staying at home waiting for the results of the shop stewards' meeting. The Communist Party anticipated changes in the situation on Monday and convened a shop stewards' meeting on Sunday. The meeting was attended by 2,000 representatives from major stores in Berlin, including some members of the Social Democratic Party and the Free Workers' Union. The speakers and the resolutions passed all stated that cooperation between the Social Democratic Party and the Communist Party was a matter of urgency. After heated debate, a resolution was passed by a majority, advocating the immediate preparation of a general strike. The two left-wing parties should form a common front and elect an executive committee, consisting of seven Communist Party members and eight Social Democratic Party members, to be responsible for directing joint activities. After the meeting ended, the resolution passed spread like wildfire throughout the working-class areas. Although independent observers do not deny that there is a radical tendency in the labor movement, they believe that the Social Democratic Party is determined to wait for the development of the Reichstag to determine its course and opposes rash action. The traditional discipline of the Social Democratic Party should be able to prevent party members from joining the Communist Party. However, the government seems to have decided to exert its energy to deal with the general strike.

Reuters, Berlin, 31st - The Communist Party's newspaper, "Die Rote Fahne," today used the large headline "To Battle" to declare war on the Hitler government. The newspaper called on all socialist groups to participate in the general strike and revealed the resolutions passed at a meeting of 2,000 labor union leaders, stating that Hitler had secretly suffered defeat under the power of our general strike, just like the collapse of the Kapp Putsch in 1920.

Chairman Chiang Arrives in Jiangxi

=Lands at Xun and Immediately Takes Special Train to Nanchang=

=Various Bandits, Hearing the News, Flee South Toward the Fujian Border=

Nanchang Correspondent, After Chairman Chiang suppressed the large Red bandit groups in Henan, Hubei, and Anhui last year, he planned to come to Jiangxi to continue supervising the suppression of the Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang bandit groups and complete the task of eradicating the Red bandits. However, due to the convening of the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee, he returned to Nanjing, so the trip was delayed. Unexpectedly, Zhu, Mao, and Peng, fearing that the National Army would launch a large-scale encirclement and suppression, took advantage of the violent Japanese invasion of Yuguan and launched a full-scale attack north from the Fujian border, capturing Jinxi, occupying Chongren, seizing Dongxiang, forcing Xianxian, attacking Fuzhou, and threatening Nanchang. The Fang Shao in northeastern Jiangxi, Li Zhu in southwestern Jiangxi, and Kong Hechong bandit groups in northwestern Jiangxi, as well as scattered bandits in various places, also launched large-scale activities to respond, as the bandits wanted to concentrate all their forces to make a desperate gamble and seize Nanwan to get out to the Yangtze River. At that time, the departments in the province guarded the Fuzhou area. All sectors also sent telegrams to the central government asking for help, urging Chiang to come to Jiangxi to supervise the suppression. It was heard that Chiang also considered the bandit disaster in Jiangxi to be of great importance to the southeast, and in order to consolidate the rear and eliminate obstacles to resisting Japan, he boarded the Chuyou warship from Nanjing at 9:00 PM on the 27th of this month, with the Xianning warship following. However, due to the shallow water, the ship traveled very slowly. It only arrived in Jiujiang on the morning of the 29th. Provincial Government Chairman Xiong Shihui, Commissioners Gong Xue, Li Dezhao, Wen Qun, Provincial Party Committee members Fan Zhengbo, Wang Guanying, and Li Zhongxiang, as well as the Jiujiang District Administrative Officer Chen, the Garrison Commander, and hundreds of people from all walks of life in Jiujiang, were all on the riverbank to welcome him. After Chairman Chiang landed and greeted the welcomers, he took a car to the Nanchang-Xunyang Railway Station to board a special train. At 10:30 AM, the special train departed from Xunyang. All members of the Provincial Party Committee and the Provincial Government accompanied him to the province. Chairman Xiong reported to Chiang on the train about the bandit suppression situation in the province, the military situation, and the political facilities, and discussed military and political matters. Chiang also met with the members of the Provincial Party Committee and the Provincial Government one by one, inquiring in detail about party affairs, politics, post-disaster relief in bandit areas, etc., and gave instructions on each report. The train stopped briefly in Dean. Dean County Chief Luo Yunpi and the county party affairs committee member led representatives from all walks of life to welcome him at the station. Chiang also met with County Chief Luo and the party affairs committee member to inquire about the local situation. The train then headed south, adding water and coal in Tubu. He Guoguang, Chief of Staff of the Joint Command of the Jiangxi, Guangdong, and Fujian Provinces, rushed from the province and boarded the train to meet Chiang. He also reported the general situation of the bandit suppression in the three provinces, the Zhu and Mao attack north, the recent military situation at the front, and asked for instructions. At 3:00 PM, the special train arrived at Niuxing Station. Senior military and political officials were all at the station to welcome him. Mass organizations such as farmers, businessmen, students, party, government, military, and police lined up in order to greet him on the riverbank. At 4:30 PM, amidst cheers from the crowd, Chiang crossed the river from the station, took a car through Zhongshan Road, and disembarked at the Science Museum. Xiong, He, and others accompanied him by car, and discussed the major plan of suppressing the Red bandits at the Science Museum. It is heard that Chiang came here specifically to suppress the Red bandits. After the military deployment, he will still have to return to Nanjing. There are rumors that he will go to Wuhan, but there is no fixed date. However, the Luo Binghui bandit group has already withdrawn from Liufang in Fuzhou to Xuhuan. The Peng Dehuai bandit group withdrew from Dongxiang. The pseudo 15th Army Group withdrew from Jinxi to Zixi. According to front-line telegrams, Chen Cheng's 11th Division recovered Jinxi on the 28th, and Li Yunjie's Division recovered Xuhuan on the 25th. The Dongxiang County Chief also telegraphed the province yesterday to report that he had returned to the county to handle post-disaster relief. It is that the bandits are again trying to avoid the real and attack the empty, shrinking back to their old nests, but the armies of Fujian Province have arrived at the Jiangxi border from northwestern Fujian to cut off the bandits' retreat, and with the southeastern Jiangxi departments, taking the form of a pincer attack, it is expected that under Chiang's unified command, they will no longer be allowed to flee here and there. (January 29)

Chairman Chiang Commends the Jiangxi Security Office

Nanchang Correspondent, The General Headquarters for the Suppression of Bandits in Hubei, Henan, and Anhui, based on the suggestion of Jin Handing, used political organizations to assist the military in suppressing bandits. It ordered the provinces with bandits to pay attention. After receiving the instruction, the Jiangxi Provincial Security Office believed that the office's political design and suppression organization were more precise than Jin Handing's proposal. In addition to implementing political orders such as reorganizing security groups, organizing teams, conducting joint defense, going deep into bandit areas, harvesting late rice, recruiting refugees, and appeasing those who were coerced and those who repented, it ordered the county chiefs of all county areas that were fully or partially occupied by bandits to secretly plan to recover them with political force, and formulated appropriate measures for each response. It ordered the counties to comply with the records. According to the above-mentioned process, it copied the instructions and reported them to the General Headquarters. It is heard that Chairman Chiang, who is also the Commander-in-Chief, gave instructions to Jiangxi yesterday, saying that the office's proposals were very correct and worthy of praise and consolation.

Huang Shao-hong and Cai Tingkai Arrive in Guangdong One After Another

=Huang Conveying the Central Government's Intentions=

=Cai Discussing National Salvation Plans=

Guangzhou Correspondent, It is heard that Huang Shao-hong, the Minister of the Interior, is here this time to negotiate with the authorities in the two Guangdong provinces. When Mr. Huang arrived in Hong Kong, Li Zongren happened to be in Hong Kong to meet with Li Jishen. He then accompanied Mr. Huang to Guangzhou. That afternoon, Li and Huang visited Chen Jitang and the Central Committee members in the Southwest. The authorities held banquets to welcome Huang. According to Mr. Huang, after arriving in Hong Kong this time, he met with Mr. Li Jishen and conveyed the central government's opinions. Mr. Li's illness has gradually improved, but there is no date for his return to the north. He also visited Hu Hanmin and discussed the current situation. Only on the evening of the 22nd did he come to Guangdong with Commander Li Zongren. His only task was to exchange opinions on the current situation and domestic affairs with the Central Committee members in the Southwest. As soon as the negotiations are completed, he will return to Guangxi. The purpose of returning to Guangxi is that Guangxi is actively handling the people's militia, so he will take the opportunity to inspect its training status. Also, Guangxi recently established a political experimental zone, and he also intends to inspect its facilities and content. The Guangxi authorities previously intended to assign him the position of director of the political experimental zone, but because of the busy affairs of the ministry, he had no time to go south to preside over it, so he still recommended Wu Tingyang to be responsible. He will return to Guangxi and stay for two weeks before returning to the north. Because the situation in Hebei is tense recently, the central government has actively prepared to deal with the Yuguan incident and plans to have a whole plan. The people of the country should work together for the country, he said. On the 23rd, Chen Jitang hosted Huang at the Taiping Restaurant, with Li Zongren, Zhang Renmin, Miao Peinan, and Huang Huabiao accompanying him. They dispersed happily until about 2:00 PM. Huang was originally scheduled to return to Guangxi at noon on the 23rd, but because there were still important matters to be discussed in Guangdong, the schedule was temporarily changed. Only Ma Junwu returned to Wuzhou first. It is heard that Huang is temporarily staying in Guangdong to exchange opinions on the current situation with Cai Tingkai. It is because Mr. Cai arrived in Hong Kong from Fuzhou by boat on the 24th and arrived in Guangzhou on the 25th. After Huang met with Mr. Cai, he scheduled to return to Guangxi around the 27th or 28th.

Cai Tingkai, the commander of the Nineteenth Route Army, recently arrived in Guangzhou from Fujian on January 23 because the military leaders of the two Guangdong provinces were gathered in Guangzhou, and Huang Shao-hong, the Minister of the Interior, also arrived in Guangdong to discuss important matters regarding the current situation. He arrived in Hong Kong on the 24th, stayed in Hong Kong for one night, and arrived in Guangzhou at 2:40 PM on the 25th. His companion was Weng Guiqing, the director of the army's office in Guangdong. After landing, Mr. Cai returned to the mansion on Daxiang Road to rest briefly and received guests. He expressed extreme indignation at the recent invasion of Yuguan by the violent Japanese. According to him, "This time the enemy captured Yuguan, attacked Jiukou, and attempted to annex Rehe, invaded Pingjin, and got an inch and wanted a mile, gradually trying to encompass Hebei and directly attack the Yangtze River. The Southwest cannot be guaranteed either. Our army has long seen through the conspiracy of the Japanese warlords, so in the Battle of Shanghai, we were not afraid of how violent the enemy was, and annihilated their fierce offensive. We declared that even if there was only one soldier left, we would not allow the enemy to succeed. The current situation is that only a war can be used to seek survival. If we continue to be negligent, the result will not be only the destruction of the country. If you look at Turkey when the national crisis was pressing and the land was shrinking day by day, its government even moved to the mountains and fought a desperate battle with the enemy, so it finally achieved its goal of revival. Now our country has not yet reached the point of danger that Turkey was in that day. If we can unite from top to bottom and use the army of the whole country to deal with the violent Japanese, the country's fortune may not be irreversible. For this reason, our army recently specially asked the central government to volunteer to go north to kill the enemy. The central government has telegraphed that it should be temporarily concentrated and await orders. Once the order is given, I will lead the ten and eight regiments of troops to the north and fight a decisive battle with the enemy again. Success or failure is not what I care about," he said. Mr. Cai has met with Huang Shao-hong, Chen Jitang, Li Zongren, and other members of the Southwest Central Committee for many times in recent days to discuss various important issues of resisting Japan and to discuss plans to eliminate the communist bandits in southern Jiangxi in the short term. It is expected that he will stay in Guangdong for a few days before returning to Fujian. (January 27)

Wuxi

Dredging of Daqiao River Implemented

Daqiao River, outside the North Gate of this county, is an important route for the Suzhou-Changzhou traffic on the canal. It is currently not very well silted, and ships often run aground. During the winter season when the water is dry, the County Chamber of Commerce convened various industries to discuss dredging methods and raise funds to organize the Daqiao River Engineering Committee, which is responsible for the construction bureau. Starting from the Taogeng and Wang Yuanlai doors along the river to the river along the sesame cake, construction of the dam began on January 24. The county government is deeply concerned that the traffic of ships will obstruct the project, and specially issued a bulletin to inform the public to facilitate the work. The section of the river has been drained by water pumps day and night, and the water has been drained. Many fish and shrimp have been caught. Yesterday, electric lights were installed in the river and more than a hundred workers were hired to start dredging. It will be completed in a few days, and the stone feet of the Daqiao Bridge will be repaired to strengthen the bridge.

Jiangsu-Jurong Road Bus Service Resumes

The Jiangsu-Jurong long-distance bus service was previously interrupted due to snow and ice. It was inconvenient to drive in the cold weather, and the number of buses was reduced. Now that the weather is gradually warming and the ice and snow have melted, the management office has decided to resume the original number of buses and operate as usual from February 1 (i.e., a total of eight buses run between Zhenjiang and Jurong). The bus timetable has been changed, i.e., the last bus from Jurong to the province has been changed to 3:40 PM to connect with the Jiangnan Bus Company.

[P Aviation Association Announcement>

Mayor Wu Serves as the Captain of the Headquarters

Lin and Wang Went to Hangzhou Yesterday to Establish a Branch

After the establishment of the China Aviation Association, No. 99 Jessfield Road was selected as the address of the association. However, the business community is in the process of closing accounts, and the repair workers are also taking a break according to custom, so the place has not yet been completely repaired. However, due to the small size of the preparatory office, it is not enough to use. Now some of the staff have moved in to work. Yesterday, a reporter from the Central News Agency interviewed Mr. Lin Wojiang, the executive director of the association, at the preparatory office to discuss the current situation of the association. The following is a transcript:

Seeking Members

Mr. Lin stated that the membership rules of this association were drafted at the beginning of the preparation stage and announced during the inaugural meeting. Recently, numerous letters have been received from various places requesting the rules and applying for membership. In this city, the Executive Committee decided yesterday (i.e., the day before yesterday) to organize a membership recruitment team, extensively gathering comrades to work together. Mayor Wu was nominated as the captain of the recruitment team, with Director Wang Rutang as the chief of staff. Therefore, all planning related to membership recruitment will be carried out through consultations between Directors Wu and Wang.

Organizing Branches

Mr. Lin continued, stating that yesterday's meeting also nominated Directors Lin Kanghou and Wang Xiaolai as preparation committee members for the Hangzhou branch. This morning (i.e., yesterday morning), the two gentlemen have already traveled together to make all arrangements. As for other regions, branches will be organized in important cities in order. Smaller areas such as counties and towns will organize sub-branches, with the ultimate goal of extending the organization's reach throughout the country. If vocational groups voluntarily collect funds to purchase aircraft, the name of the group will be used as the name of the aircraft, and the association will handle the custody and use. Currently, in addition to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the chambers of commerce in Qingdao and Wuxi have also contacted the association with letters expressing their intention to initiate fundraising for aircraft purchases.

Manufacturing Aircraft

In the future, after raising a considerable amount of funds, the first step will be to order various aircraft from foreign countries. The second step will be to establish factories for self-manufacturing. Raw materials such as steel and wood are still produced in our country, and the required quantities are also small. The most difficult and lacking aspects are the manufacturing of engines and the required refined steel, as our country lacks large-scale manufacturing factories for both. In the future, we should actively construct them to achieve self-sufficiency.

Publishing Publications

After Mr. Lin finished speaking, he presented a book published by the association, "Comparison of Air Forces of Major Powers." The book, written by Mr. Lin, details the strength of the air forces of various countries to show the efforts and strategies of various countries in aviation construction, serving as a reference for the people of the country. In this high tide of saving the country through aviation, it is indeed a good guide. Regarding the construction of our country's air force, it does not focus on manufacturing aircraft carriers but emphasizes airships and, even more so, on cultivating talents for civil and commercial aviation as reserve combatants for the air force. Four Patriotic Children

Saving Candy Money to Donate for Aircraft

Mayor Greatly Admired Upon Receiving Letter

Various agencies and organizations in this city held an Aviation Save-the-Nation Propaganda Week at the end of last month, in order to make the general public aware that national defense should focus on aviation equipment, and to encourage them to actively donate funds to assist the government in purchasing aircraft to strengthen national defense. It is reported that four children residing at No. 71, Lane 201, Luban Road—Fang Xiaoruo, an 11-year-old boy; Chen Yingzeng, a 14-year-old boy; Dong Ying, a 14-year-old girl; and Fang Yunying, a 12-year-old girl—sent a letter to Mayor Wu, proposing that children voluntarily donate to manufacture a Shanghai Children's Aircraft to show that children's patriotism is no less than that of adults. They donated four silver dollars saved from their usual candy money to the municipal government for the purchase of aircraft. Mayor Wu deeply appreciated their intention and specially replied to the four children, praising them greatly. He also forwarded the four silver dollars to the Aviation Association for receipt. The letters from the four children and the mayor's reply are transcribed below:

Letter from the Four Children

Our beloved Mayor, the day before yesterday, we heard your speech on saving the nation through aviation on the radio, and we were deeply moved. The barbaric Japanese imperialism, which does not abide by justice, seized our three northeastern provinces last year, killed thousands of our compatriots in Shanghai, and destroyed countless houses. This year, they seized our Shanhaiguan. Now they want our Beiping, Tianjin, and other places. We should resist desperately. But we children cannot go to the front line to kill the bandits, but we should also bear some responsibility. I now respectfully propose to the Mayor to persuade all children in Shanghai to save candy money to buy a military bomber to fight Japan. Now, we four children have gathered together, and each of us has donated the candy money given to us by our mothers, totaling four silver dollars, and asked the Mayor to vigorously promote it. If a "Shanghai Children's Aircraft" is successfully built, then our China will surely be saved. Beloved Mayor, we hope you will work hard for us children with all your heart, and wish you courage and health. Attached are four silver dollars. Eleven-year-old boy Fang Xiaoruo, fourteen-year-old boy Chen Yingzeng, fourteen-year-old girl Dong Ying, twelve-year-old girl Fang Yunying.

Mayor's Reply

Reading your letter makes me very happy. Your innocent and fervent spirit of loving the nation and saving the country is not only worthy of admiration but also proves that our nation's future still has infinite hope. Your support for and practice of saving the nation through aviation can not only serve as a model for children across the country but also as a standard for people across the country. We will do our best to promote your proposal to persuade all children in Shanghai to save candy money and donate to purchase aircraft. We plan to publish the letter in newspapers so that children throughout the city and the people of the country can be excited and launch a grand and widespread aviation save-the-nation movement. The donation of four yuan you sent has been handed over to the Aviation Association, and the receipt will be sent directly by the association. Wishing you health and hard work. Wu Tiecheng.

Origin of the Lake Society's Aircraft Fundraising

Wu Zhihui and Others Initiate Fundraising

"Chen Shenfu" Fighter Plane

Chen Yingshi's eldest son, Shenfu, died in a training plane crash on September 9 last year at the Jianqiao Bridge in Hangzhou. He Yingqin, Minister of Military Affairs, and others initiated a memorial service at the Lake Society on Guizhou Road on the 18th of last month. At that time, Wu Zhihui, a member of the Central Supervisory Committee, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, and others proposed setting up a memorial and raising funds to purchase a fighter plane named "Chen Shenfu," and all the representatives present would be the initiators to leave a memorial. This was unanimously approved, and all members of the Lake Society were entrusted to be the preparatory committee members of the fundraising committee for purchasing fighter planes in memory of Chen Shenfu. A reporter from Huadong News met with Bao Juxiang, a member of the preparatory committee, yesterday. According to him, this matter is now underway, including rules and regulations for fundraising. All the origins have been drafted by Pan Gongzhan and Shen Youxin and passed by the standing committee. They will be submitted for discussion at the executive meeting to be convened soon to engage in fundraising and purchasing. The origin is recorded below: Chen Shenfu was the eldest son of the revolutionary martyr Mr. Yingshi. He was born intelligent and had extraordinary ambitions from a young age. During the January 28th Incident last year, he was indignant at the weakness of national defense and the invasion of short bandits. He believed that without an air force, it would not be enough to defend against foreign aggression. Therefore, he applied to the Jianqiao Aviation School, planning to serve the country in the future and continue his father's legacy to fulfill his aspirations to serve the country. Unexpectedly, on the second day of school, he accompanied Instructor Shi Manniu on a training flight and died tragically. His great ambition was not fulfilled, and he died first, which is deeply regrettable. My colleagues are aware that recently, the important fortress of Yuguan has been ravaged again, and the violent flames of the tyrannical Japan are becoming more and more obvious. They increasingly feel the urgent need for an air force. Therefore, they will purchase an aircraft as a sign of remembrance and to comfort the loyal soul. All gentlemen are no less patriotic than others, especially when the national crisis has not yet ended. They will surely be happy to follow suit. Please generously donate as much as possible, so that you can gather strength and realize it as soon as possible. You will see the flying wings in the sky, startling the enemy, and the Yellow Dragon will drink heartily, and open the flowers of revolution everywhere. The name will be passed down through the ages, and the story will be equal to the title bridge. The sound will be heard in five continents. With the same ambition to love the country, this action will not only be a slight comfort to the spirit of the martyrs, but also a representation of the will of the people. This is the beginning.

Wu Chaoshu Discusses Recent International Events

Entering Beijing Today

A reporter from the Central News Agency visited Dr. Wu Chaoshu, a member of the Central Committee, at his residence yesterday morning. During the conversation, he shared many opinions related to recent international issues. They are recorded as follows:

Mandate Rule

According to Mr. Wu, there are several small islands in the South Pacific that used to belong to Germany. Although they do not have abundant products, they are strategically important because they are located at the crossroads of sea routes. Since the end of the European War, the major powers divided and seized Germany's overseas colonies at the peace conference. The small islands in the area were entrusted to Japan by the League of Nations, and the League of Nations stipulated the regulations for the mandated territory. The main point was that no military facilities should be established in the mandated territory. Since Japan took over, due to the above-mentioned restrictions, it improved the ports in the mandated territory. Since the outbreak of the Eastern Province Incident the year before last, the League of Nations received reports of Japan's military installations in the area. Before the truth was verified, it was inconvenient to comment. If it is true, this is a clear and arbitrary violation of the League of Nations' regulations by Japan, endangering peace in the Far East. I believe that the League of Nations has the right to revoke its mandate. If Japan withdraws from the League of Nations, whether its mandated territory will also be revoked is a question that requires very detailed research, because there is no precedent to refer to.

Sino-Russian Situation

After Japan seized the Northeast, it made every effort to expand its power, causing the Soviet Union to be wary. A conflict of interests is inevitable. However, observing the attitude of the Soviet Union, it is quite patient and seems unwilling to cause unexpected changes as a result. But what will be the trend between the two countries in the future? It depends on 1. the degree of Japan's invasion of China, 2. the degree of Soviet Russia's patience, and 3. the extent to which Soviet Russia's own interests are violated by Japan.

US-Russian Resumption of Diplomatic Relations

The rumor that the United States and Russia will resume diplomatic relations has been circulating for some time. The strong advocacy of Senator Borah, a famous American senator, for recognizing Soviet Russia has won the sympathy of the American government and the public. Borah has long advocated the resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia. In this critical period, there is a possibility of rapid realization. The American authorities have always expressed dissatisfaction with Japan's aggressive actions. Their attitude is the same as that of Soviet Russia. The future trend of Japan and the United States depends on the extent to which Japan infringes upon the interests of the United States itself.

War Debt Problem

The key to the world-shaking war debt problem lies in the attitude of U.S. President-elect Roosevelt, which is closely watched by the world. Roosevelt recently stated that he is willing to negotiate with various countries and hopes that various countries will give the United States commercial conveniences. The United Kingdom is prepared to send important officials to the United States to discuss and resolve the payment issue. Whether it will be reduced or waived, or whether another method of repayment will be found is difficult to predict. In short, I deeply hope that this matter can be resolved as soon as possible.

Anglo-Japanese Secret Agreement

There were rumors that the United Kingdom and Japan had an understanding during the Shanghai ceasefire last year. Whether it is true or not, I dare not say. But before the investigation is clear, we are unwilling to criticize it.

Entering Beijing Today

Mr. Wu continued, stating that he had proposed at the Third Plenary Session to establish popular opinion organs in various provinces and counties, which was approved by the conference. He was also elected as one of the drafting members of the National Political Council organization regulations. He plans to go to Beijing tomorrow (i.e., today) to attend the first meeting of the drafting committee on Thursday and return to Shanghai in two or three days.

Shanghai Electric Power Company Will Issue Bonds

HSBC Bank and Others Organize a Syndicated Underwriting

Yesterday, HSBC Bank in this port announced that the bank is underwriting 33 million taels of Shanghai Electric Power Company's 5.5% first mortgage bonds and has formed a syndicate with Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Wan Guo Savings Society, Liann Yangxing, and Xinfeng Yangxing, etc. At present, 18 million taels have been identified, and the remaining 15 million taels will be issued in the market in the near future. The actual receipt for this bond is 96, with accrued interest paid. The combined principal and interest of each 100 yuan can get 5.75% interest. As for the reason why the Electric Power Company is issuing corporate bonds this time, it is because after the company purchased the Electrical Department of the Public Works Bureau in 1929, the purchase price was 82 million taels, and it was agreed to pay it in batches. The repayment will be cleared by December 30 this year, and all company assets will be mortgaged. At present, the company has paid 56,693,910 taels for the purchase price and 12,991,513.22 taels for interest. There is still a purchase price of 24,306,090 taels to be paid in full this year. At the same time, capital has also been increased by 16,000,000 taels in expanding equipment. If combined with the purchase price paid, the company has invested 72,000,000 taels. However, this investment of 72 million taels is currently only the guarantee for the remaining purchase price of more than 24 million taels and its interest. Therefore, the company specially consulted with the Public Works Bureau in accordance with the original contract terms to recover the original collateral and replace it with the guarantee of HSBC Bank. At the same time, the company's exclusive rights and real estate within the Public Concession were transferred and mortgaged to HSBC Bank as collateral for the bank's guarantee of the remaining purchase price and the issuance of 33 million taels of bonds. This method has been approved by the Public Works Bureau, and a formal contract can be signed in the near future. Once the procedures are completed, the company can use the bond income to repay the Public Works Bureau. At the same time, it can use the remaining funds as capital. In this way, the bond interest rate is relatively lower and short-term debt is transformed into long-term corporate bonds, which also greatly benefits the company's financial position.

Page 16

Japanese Goods Invade the Yellow River Coast

Since our country has been resisting Japanese goods, it has been difficult for the Japanese to mix them in at the commercial ports. Recently, they have changed their strategy and are selling them along the Yellow River to the interior of China, using traitors to import a lot. Yesterday, a friend who runs an import and export business came to Shanghai from Huaihai. The reporter met him at the hotel and received a detailed account of the situation of Japanese goods entering the Yellow River coast. It is relayed as follows:

Departing from Dalian　The source of Japanese goods is all shipped from Dalian, divided into parts and wholesale in two types. They are rebranded and disguised as domestic goods, colluding with a private shipping company established by a certain Lu person in Dalian, promising huge profits. At least four or five thousand pieces are shipped out every month, all of which are ordered to be transported to the Shijiusuo area between Qingdao and Haizhou, where they are unloaded and then transferred to another boat for sale in the interior.

Sailing Ships for Sales　Shijiusuo has no customs checkpoints. The Japanese secretly set up warehouses there, agreeing on more than a dozen sailing ships. As soon as the Japanese goods are loaded, they are repackaged into large and small packages and carried out by the sailing ships along the Yellow River to various villages and forts along the river for sale. Because there are no donations and taxes, the price of goods has fallen to two or three percent of the cost. The people benefit from their low prices, so sales are booming.

Post Office to Offer Telegraphic Money Orders Immediately

The Shanghai Postal Administration has received an order from the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau of the Ministry of Communications to establish a new type of telegraphic money order to expedite public remittances, which will be available from February 1, 1933. The procedures for this type of money order are as follows: (1) Direct Telegraphic Money Order (transmitted only by telegraph): Initially, remittance receipts will be limited to various postal administrations and a number of first- and second-class post offices. Indirect Telegraphic Money Orders can be sent to most exchange bureaus nationwide. These indirect telegraphic money orders will be transmitted by telegraph to the post office nearest to the paying office that handles direct telegraphic money orders, and then mailed by that office to the paying office. However, the public should note that indirect telegraphic money orders are only advantageous in certain circumstances, specifically when the paying office is far from the remitting office. Therefore, all bureau chiefs have been instructed to inform remitters if a regular money order would be faster. (2) In addition to the regular money order fee, a telegraphic money order will incur a telegraph fee calculated by the number of words, plus a telegraphic transfer fee of 2.5 per mille of the remittance amount. The remitter should provide the recipient's name and address in detail to facilitate prompt payment. (3) After the remitter has paid the remittance and fees to the post office, the post office will issue a receipt for the remitter to keep. The remittance will then be telegraphed to the recipient by the remitting office or via a transferring office. (4) If the recipient of a telegraphic money order cannot prove their identity, payment can be made with a guarantor. For all other details, please inquire at your nearest post office.

The Qian Zhuang (Traditional Chinese Bank) After Year-End Closing

To Improve Business by Emulating Bank Practices

Profitable Despite Impact of War

First Meeting of Member Representatives Tomorrow

After completing the year-end closing for the 21st year of the Republic, the Qian Zhuang in both the northern and southern parts of Shanghai resumed business on the day before yesterday, starting to issue account books and improve business by emulating bank practices. Despite the impact of the war last year, fortunately, all were profitable. The details are as follows:

Improving Business: Qian Zhuang businesses have traditionally focused on lending based on credit and have operated in this way for a long time. Starting in 1933, in order to meet the needs of various sectors, each Zhuang will emulate bank practices, adding departments for mortgage loans, factory loans, trusts, remittances, savings, etc., in addition to existing services. The first to implement this will be the Fuyuan Zhuang, managed by Qin Runqing, chairman of the Qian Zhuang Association. The Yintai Zhuang, managed by Ma Sicang and Lin Ruiting, has decided to move to the old site of the Fuyuan Zhuang on Ningbo Road next month and will also emulate bank practices.

Profits of Each Zhuang: A reporter from Xin Sheng She interviewed a member of the Qian Zhuang Association yesterday, who stated that since the September 18th Incident in 1931, all industries have been affected. Qian Zhuang businesses, which primarily rely on credit lending, were bound to face danger. For caution, each Zhuang immediately implemented a contraction policy and carefully issued loans. Since the January 28th Incident, all industries have further declined. Fortunately, the Qian Zhuang had already shrunk in size after the September 18th Incident, so the impact was relatively small. After the year-end closing for the 21st year of the Republic, all Zhuang had profits, ranging from 5,000 to 150,000 taels, with the average around 40,000 to 50,000 taels.

Start Issuing Account Books: The new and old Qian Zhuang in the northern and southern markets that have resumed business in 1933, including 62 in the northern market such as the Huihua She Yuan, and 5 that have not entered the Yuan Zi Hao (brand name), such as the Dingshen Zhuang; and 5 in the southern market such as the Huihua Zhengxiang Zhuang, and 5 that have not entered the Yuan Zi Hao, such as the Yuanfeng Zhuang, totaling 77. Those that have not yet resumed business are the Xin Tonghang Huihua Tongqing Zhuang and the Lao Tonghang Huihua Anyu Zhuang, which are scheduled to resume business next month. The Qian Zhuang that have resumed business started issuing account books (i.e., opening accounts) on the day before yesterday, to be completed by February 9 (i.e., the Lantern Festival).

First General Assembly: After the Qian Zhuang in the northern and southern markets resumed business on the day before yesterday, the Qian Zhuang Association has scheduled its first general assembly of member representatives for the 22nd year of the Republic for 3 AM on February 2 at the Qian Zhuang Market on Ningbo Road to discuss various matters after the resumption of business.

Fengpu Ship Out of Danger

Arrival in Shanghai Possible Tomorrow

The Changjiang-class Fengpu ship of the Sanbei Shipping Company, which sailed from Hankou to Shanghai on the 23rd of last month, ran aground near Jiujiang. After a ship was dispatched from Hankou for rescue, it was immediately out of danger. Unexpectedly, the ship continued sailing downstream and ran aground again near Tai Zi Ji in Anqing at 9 PM on the 29th. The ship owner rescued it again. At that time, the Qingpu ship happened to pass by, and it was towed out of danger at high tide at noon the next day. The company received a telegram yesterday. Whether the ship's hull is damaged or not will only be known after the ship arrives in Shanghai for inspection. It is estimated that the ship will arrive tomorrow.

County-Administered Deed Tax: Owners to Pay Directly to Bank

Effective February 1

The Shanghai County Government has received an instruction from the Jiangsu Provincial Government, stating in brief: It is noted that the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Public Debt Fund Management Committee has submitted a report proposing changes to the collection and payment of deed tax in order to rectify the deed tax and consolidate the credit of the construction debt fund. When people pay deed tax, the county bureau will first issue a notice indicating the amount of tax due, and the taxpayer will first go to a designated bank or an agent Qian Zhuang to obtain a receipt, and then submit it to the county bureau to process the deed. The tax payment notice and receipt form have been submitted to the provincial government and have been amended, discussed, and approved by the Departments of Finance and Construction. Now, the committee has reported that the designated bank or agent Qian Zhuang for collecting and paying deed tax has been negotiated and agreed upon, and it has been decided that February 1, 1933, will be the date to start collecting the money. Please notify all county bureaus to comply. In addition to the notice and instruction, a proclamation and measures, as well as a list of designated banks or Qian Zhuang, are hereby promulgated. After receiving the order, the county government has, in addition to posting the proclamation for public knowledge, instructed the Finance Bureau and all district chiefs to comply accordingly.

Silk Industry Bank Recruitment of Trainees

The Shanghai Silk Industry Bank, located at 64 Hankou Road, is experiencing rapid business growth and has recently established four new major business initiatives. As a result, the existing staff is insufficient, and the bank plans to recruit trainees to assist. The bank has set the registration period from February 5th to February 15th, 1933. Applicants, regardless of gender, must be high school graduates or possess an equivalent education. Those wishing to apply must bring a two-inch half-length photograph and submit a completed application form and cover letter in both Chinese and English to the bank's document section. After a review, qualified candidates will be notified of the examination date.
