Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Chinese Children's Welfare Association

Adoption of This Year's Association Work Plan

Election of President, Committee Members, and Honorary Directors

The Chinese Children's Welfare Association was established in the spring of 1928 by individuals such as Kong Xiangxi, Kuang Fuzhao, and Gao Fengchi. It has been almost five years since its founding. The association's work, including child protection, child relief, child health, child research, as well as orphanages, nurseries, and children's clinics, has been practical and achieved significant results, widely recognized by the public. The association recently held its fourth annual meeting at the YMCA Zhongshan Hall, located at 20 Museum Road. A summary of the proceedings is provided below.

Attendees

Qian Zhenya, Li Yuanxin, Mr. and Mrs. Wu Zhijian, Jia Xiyan, Gu Xingqing, Yin Guanzhi, Chen Lengseng, Fischer, Ellis, Miss Barger, Miss White Rock Bay, Miss Wu Yuxin, Wu Weide, Chen Tiesheng, Wang Yi, Chen Zhengfan, Zhang Yueru, Xuan Bokun, and dozens of others.

Chairman's Address

The meeting began with an opening address by the chairman, Kong Xiangxi (represented by Qian Zhenya), who stated, "Since its establishment, the association has worked hard to promote children's welfare, starting from fundamental planning. It provides relief and protection to abused children, promotes the well-being of ordinary children in various ways, and strives to cultivate them into useful talents for the nation and society in the future. This undertaking is extensive and involves numerous tasks. It requires the concerted efforts of all members and the awakening of the nation's awareness of children's welfare to jointly promote this child welfare movement for the revival of the nation." The chairman then read the annual meeting declaration, which was unanimously approved and is recorded below.

Declaration of the General Assembly

The association is about to complete its fifth year of establishment. In the past five years, with the support of domestic pioneers in child welfare and the assistance of international colleagues, we have developed gradually and expanded steadily. We have managed to carry out several initiatives, such as child protection, child relief, child health, child research, and facilities such as child welfare gardens, orphanages, and clinics. We also requested the National Government to designate April 4th as Children's Day to draw the attention of the entire nation, hoping that this child welfare undertaking can be promoted to all cities, towns, and villages across the country, so that every household and everyone knows that children are the future masters of the country and should work together to nurture them, so that 120 million children can achieve complete happiness and full development. Our association is willing to unite with people across the country to create a new environment and a new society for children, thereby restoring the highest position of our Chinese nation and promoting the unparalleled glory of our Chinese nation. Children are the inheritors of the nation, and children's welfare is the fundamental work for national revival. We hope that compatriots across the country will use their full strength to promote this cause, expand the child welfare movement, and seek happiness for children who are deprived of care, education, and support, in order to lay a new foundation for our nation. At this critical time of national crisis and the pressing threat of powerful neighbors, our colleagues feel the weight of our responsibilities even more. We must work together with people across the country, refine our spirit, strive for self-improvement, and accomplish this great mission. This is our declaration.

Work Report

Secretary Wu Weide then reported on the association's work over the past year, including providing relief to children affected by the floods in Wuhan and Jiangbei, establishing the Shanghai War Zone Orphan Temporary Orphanage, holding the April 4th Children's Day celebrations, protecting abused children, caring for unsupported children, establishing a Children's Welfare Group for the children of workers in the Yangshupu area, setting up two children's disease clinics in Zhabei and Yangshupu, publishing the Children's Welfare Monthly, publishing a collection of children's songs, and other promotional booklets. The general assembly then approved the association's work plan for the year as follows:

Work Plan

(1) Hold large-scale Children's Day celebrations; (2) Prepare to convene a national conference of child welfare leaders; (3) Promote the establishment of local child welfare branches; (4) Fundraise for regular and special expenses; (5) Change the Education Department to the Relief Department; (6) Change the Social Education Department to the Publicity Department; A. Send personnel to give lectures in various locations; B. Publish the Modern Parents Monthly; C. Publish the Child Welfare Series of small books; D. Other promotional activities; (7) The Research Department initiates a family education research association; (8) The Health Department prints and distributes health-related materials; (9) Promote wholesome entertainment for children; (10) Progress of the Model Orphanage in the Capital: A. Measure and plan the usage of the site address; B. Invite engineers to draw up architectural plans for the orphanage in preparation for construction; C. Fundraise for construction costs. Subsequently, the new budget for the year was approved, and new officers were elected as follows:

Newly Elected Officers

(President) Kong Xiangxi, (First Vice President) Luo Yunyan, (Second Vice President) Ms. Ding Shujing, (Treasurer) Lin Kanghou, (Deputy Treasurer) Sun Ruihuang, (Secretary) Chen Heqin, (Executive Committee Members) Zhu Lide, Li Tingan, Mrs. Li Jinlun, Hu Xuanming, Mrs. Guo Shun, Guo Yunguan, Fei Wusheng, Fei Si, Zhao Jinqing, Le Lingsheng, Mrs. Liu Zhanen, Mrs. Zhang Xuelou, Kuang Fuzhao, (Honorary Directors) Chairman of the National Government Lin, Shanghai Mayor Wu, Wang Yiting, Wang Zhengting, Cai Yuanpei, Xiong Xiling, Pan Gongzhan, Wang Xiaolai, Niu Huisheng, Zhu Jingnong, General Zhu Qinglan, Sir Ho Tung, Wu Jingxiong, Yu Rizhang, Li Zushen, Qu Wenliu, Hu Wenhu, Hu Yike, Tao Zhihxing, Gao Fengchi, Ma Yingbiao, Zhang Boling, Zhang Jingjiang, Xu Shiying, Yan Yangchu, He Hengfu, Cheng Bolu, Huang Hanzhi, Yong Jianqiu, Cheng Jingyi, Wen Lanting, Zhong Rongguang, (Honorary Legal Counsel) Xue Pianbi.

Representative Speeches

After the election of officers, representatives from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Chen Lengseng; the Public Security Bureau, Yin Guanzhi; and Dr. Ba from Hangzhou Guangji Hospital, spoke in turn, expressing their admiration for the association and their hope that it would strive to move forward and seek happiness for children across the country, so as to lay the foundation for the nation. Finally, the meeting adjourned after refreshments.

Shanghai Municipal Council's 15th Concert

The Shanghai Municipal Council's fifteenth symphony concert will be held this Sunday, February 5th, at 9:15 a.m. The venue remains the Carlton Theatre. The program will include selections from Wagner and Tschaikonsky, as well as three sections of Falla's "The Three-Cornered Hat" ballet.

New Swindling Tricks Exposed on Ocean Liners

| Professional swindlers of Western tableware apprehended |

In the past month, new scams have been occurring on Shanghai ocean liners. Two swindlers specialize in defrauding valuables from the dining rooms of various ships. Many have been fooled. Yesterday, the chief mate of the Haizhou steamer apprehended the criminals and turned them over to the Water Police Station. Our reporter investigated and presents the details below.

Swindling Lianxing's Goods: The swindlers consist of three or four people, with two operating each time. They specifically target newly arrived ocean liners. The Lianxing steamer of the Zhaoxing Company, arriving in Shanghai from Dalian and Tianjin, was targeted on January 30th. Two swindlers, one dressed in a short blue cloth jacket and the other in Western attire, appearing quite affluent, approached the Lianxing steamer to see the supervisor. The supervisor was unavailable, so chief mate Li Jin received them. The swindlers claimed to be the supervisor of a certain ship, produced a business card with a title, and stated that they needed to borrow Western tableware due to a shortage for entertaining guests on board. They also falsely claimed to be acting on behalf of a certain gentleman and that they were acquainted with the supervisor of the Lianxing steamer. Li Jin, unsuspecting, lent them the items. When the supervisor returned, he denied knowing the individuals and, upon inquiring with the supposed friend, confirmed that no one had been sent to borrow the items. It was then realized that they had been swindled.

Report to the Navigation Society: After being deceived, Li Jin reported the incident to the Navigation Society, a gathering place for sailors, and posted a notice warning all sailors not to be deceived by such incidents. The society also informed its members, instructing them to detain any swindlers who approached the ship and hand them over to the authorities to prevent harm to other ocean liners.

Swindling Haizhou Steamer Again: The Haizhou steamer of the Hezhong Company returned to Shanghai from Dabu and docked at River Tube No. 23. In the afternoon of the previous day, two swindlers arrived at the ship, seeking to see the supervisor. However, all the crew members were ashore, leaving only a few stewards. They were told that no one was on board and that they should return the next day (January 31st). The two swindlers returned by sampan at 10 a.m. the following day, seeking to see the supervisor. Chief mate Li Dacai met with them and inquired about their business. They claimed to be from the Anxing steamer, seeking to retrieve the Western tableware borrowed by the Haizhou steamer from the Anxing steamer's supervisor on January 26th of the previous month. Li Dacai, having received notice from the public association, recognized them as swindlers. Without revealing his suspicion, he played along while devising a plan to capture them.

Two Swindlers Captured: Li Dacai stated that if they wanted to retrieve the borrowed items, they should enter the supervisor's office and collect them themselves. Overjoyed, the two swindlers entered the supervisor's office and collected countless Western utensils, including knives, forks, bowls, and plates, claiming they belonged to the Anxing steamer and instructing the other swindler to carry them away. Unbeknownst to them, Li Dacai had signaled for their sampan to leave and summoned the Water Police. The two swindlers were apprehended, the stolen goods were recovered, and they were handed over to the police for severe punishment. Li Dacai also reported the case to the police station and presented the stolen goods, which bore the Haizhou steamer's markings. The two swindlers were left speechless. The case of swindling on ocean liners, which had been ongoing for a month, was finally exposed yesterday morning.

Two Courts Burned Confiscated Drugs and Reactionary Books and Newspapers

The Shanghai First Special District Local Court regularly burns confiscated drugs, such as opium, raw opium, opium paste, smoking paraphernalia, red pills, morphine, cocaine, heroin, and the like, every three months to demonstrate its determination to combat drugs. Yesterday was another scheduled burning. The burning location was still the Tongren Fuyuan Tang Yizhongdi (cemetery) to the south of the court. The drugs burned were those confiscated during the three months of October, November, and December of last year. The variety was extensive, and the quantity was considerable. The estimated value was even more significant. Court President Guo Yunguan took the burning of these drugs very seriously. He selected staff members to supervise the court clerks as they transported each item from the confiscated goods warehouse to the burning site. In addition to sending letters to various municipal agencies and legal associations, inviting them to send representatives to supervise, he also dispatched several court investigators to the site to oversee the clerks' work. Inside and outside the site, court police were ordered to maintain strict order. At 2:00 p.m., the burning began. Each item was first inspected before being thrown into the flames and doused with salt and kerosene to prevent any irregularities. The burning continued until sunset. President Guo also issued a notice to inform the public.

Furthermore, the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court periodically gathers and publicly burns reactionary books, newspapers, and other printed materials confiscated by the court. As a considerable amount of such materials had accumulated, requiring immediate disposal, Court President Shen Jiayi selected yesterday afternoon as the date to burn them. The burning site was located in the Yizhongdi to the south of the court. In addition to sending invitations to various agencies and organizations to send representatives to observe the proceedings, he also dispatched several court investigators to the site to oversee the clerks' work. The materials burned included a large quantity of certain communist books, followed by certain reactionary newspapers. In a short time, they were reduced to ashes.

Midnight Robbery in Dark Alley, Police Officer Dies in Line of Duty, Two Robbers Captured

Gunshots Suddenly Ring Out Near the Great World

Police Officer Wang Weigui Dies While Capturing Robbers

Two Robbers Captured by Patrol Team

At around 2:00 a.m. yesterday, outside the wall of the Great World amusement park on Avenue de Messimy in the French Concession, gunshots suddenly rang out. Initially, residents thought it was firecrackers being set off for the Lunar New Year and paid little attention. However, the cries of "robbery" grew louder, causing chaos on the street. It was then realized that armed robbers were resisting arrest. As a result, a Chinese police officer was shot in the head, his brains splattered, and he died shortly after being taken to the hospital. Two robbers were captured at the scene. Details are provided below.

Robbers Strip Clothing in Dark Alley: Zhu Chunlin, a 27-year-old Wuxi merchant residing at No. 1 Fuxing Lane, Avenue Bai Le, French Concession, went to the Great World amusement park with his roommate, Qiu Jinchang, on the evening of the fifth day of the Lunar New Year (traditionally known as the day of the God of Wealth). They returned home at around 1:00 a.m. yesterday. However, as they were passing the Huanghe Road entrance behind the Slaughterhouse Company on Rue Glocque, three robbers suddenly emerged from a dark alley. Two were wearing long robes, and one was wearing Western attire. The one in Western attire pulled out a pistol and threatened Zhu, robbing him of a gray gabardine jacket and one dollar and twenty cents in cash.

Robber in Western Attire Fires from Behind: After obtaining the stolen goods, the three robbers headed north along Avenue de Messimy. Zhu, unwilling to let them get away, secretly followed behind. Due to the late hour, he did not see any patrols along the way. He followed them to the side gate of the Huangjin Grand Theatre on Avenue Edward VII, where he saw Police Officer Wang Weigui (29 years old, from Yancheng), No. 614 of the Mecan Police Station, on duty. Zhu immediately approached him and reported the robbery. The police officer, upon hearing the report, bravely stepped forward to block their path and search them. As the police officer was searching the first robber, the robber in Western attire at the rear suddenly drew a pistol and fired at the police officer. The bullet struck the police officer's right forehead, and he collapsed to the ground.

One Robber Ultimately Captured After Pursuit: After the police officer collapsed, his brains splattered. The three robbers took the opportunity to flee east along Avenue de la Route. At that time, a special patrol team from the police station happened to be inspecting pedestrians in the area. Upon hearing the gunshots, they knew something was wrong and rushed to the scene. They saw two robbers fleeing for their lives and immediately surrounded them, drawing their pistols and chasing after them. As a result, one robber was captured at the intersection of Xixinqiao Street and taken to the police station. The injured Police Officer Wang was immediately taken to Renji Hospital by car. However, his skull was shattered, and he died upon arrival.

Robber in Western Attire Ultimately Falls into the Hands of the Law: After being taken to the police station, the captured robber, after being interrogated, confessed his name as Yu Tingrong, 33 years old, from Ningbo. He also revealed that his accomplices were hiding in Room 54, 5th floor, Siming Hotel, No. 96 Xizilaihuo Street. Superintendent Jin Jiulin of the special task force, along with detectives Zhang Ziquan, Bao Daogui, Cai Mianzhang, and others, rushed to the scene to search. They successfully apprehended the robber in Western attire, who confessed his name as Zheng Ziming, 19 years old, from Ningbo. A six-round revolver and forty-two bullets were found in the room. The barrel of the gun still showed signs of recent firing. Both were taken to the police station for detention.

Two Robbers Escorted to Court for Questioning: After Police Officer Wang Weigui died in the hospital, detective Wang Licheng was dispatched by the police station to take the body to the mortuary at Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall. At 11:00 a.m., the police station escorted Yu and Zheng to the Second Special District Court, where Criminal Court Judge Wang Wangxu presided over the trial in Criminal Court No. 1. First, police station lawyer Yao Zhaodi stood up and presented the case, stating that the case was still under investigation and requesting a postponement. He then presented the pistol, bullets, and stolen coat as evidence. Next, Zhu Chunlin, the victim, testified about the circumstances of the robbery. When questioned, the first defendant, Yu Tingrong, admitted without hesitation that he, Zheng, and Tang Awu, who was still at large, had committed the robbery and that he had shot and killed Police Officer Wang Weigui while resisting arrest. The second defendant, Zheng Ziming, also confessed that, in a moment of panic, Tang Awu ordered him to fire at the police officers to scare them away. Afterwards, he returned to the hotel and hid the pistol in the room. He was about to escape when he was apprehended by a detective on the second floor.

Autopsy of the Tragically Deceased Police Officer: Judge Wang then asked where the pistol came from. The answer was: "Tang Awu gave it to me." Judge Wang reviewed the confession and ordered them to be taken back into custody, rescheduling the trial for February 21st. He also instructed the Chief of the Criminal Affairs Division of the General Police Station to request the Second Special Court to appoint Prosecutor Deng Baosun to conduct an autopsy on the body at 11:30 a.m., accompanied by forensic doctor Jiang Xuan and clerk Peng. After the detectives reported the circumstances, the father of the deceased, Wang Gusheng, testified that the deceased was his son and that he had been tragically shot and killed by robbers. He requested justice. Deng Jun obtained a statement and ruled that Wang Weigui had died from being shot in the head by robbers. The body was released to the father for burial after he signed a pledge. After the police station completed the autopsy, the body was photographed and taken for burial.

Police Station to Provide Generous Compensation to the Deceased's Family: Police Officer Wang's home was located at No. 14 Qing'an Lane, Caojiawan. His father, Wang Gusheng, was nearly seventy years old and depended on the deceased for support. He was devastated by his son's tragic death. Police Officer Wang had served in the police force for only a little over a year and was known for his diligence. His death in the line of duty was deeply mourned by the head of the police station. It was reported that, in addition to raising funds to help the family with funeral expenses, a request had been submitted to the Chief of Police to provide generous compensation to console the deceased and serve as an example for the future.

Zhang Shaoyi Convicted of Embezzling Opium

| Sentenced to Four Years and Six Months Imprisonment and a Fine of Two Thousand Yuan |

Zhang Shaoyi, the director of the Receipt and Escort Section of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's Third Division, and police officers Ji Asi and Wu Deyu were investigated by the Shanghai Local Court for embezzling confiscated opium. After the prosecutor filed a public indictment, Judge Hu Jingqing was assigned to review the case. After the debate concluded, the court issued its verdict yesterday, sentencing Zhang Shaoyi to four years and six months of imprisonment and a fine of two thousand yuan for the crime of embezzling opium. Ji Asi and Wu Deyu were found not guilty. Zhang Shaoyi appealed the verdict, and the prosecutor also appealed the not-guilty verdict for Ji Asi and Wu Deyu.

The Last Grand Battle of the World's Number One Chess Master

| Two wins, three losses, and six draws |

Dr. Euwe, who won the world chess championship in South America in 1927, held his final grand battle last night at the Xiqing Gymnasium, playing without seeing the board. At noon, Xie Xiaxun invited Chinese and Western chess masters to a luncheon at the Zhongshe Restaurant. Dr. Euwe stated that he had traveled from Europe and the Americas to China, visiting over thirty countries. He needed to return to the Chicago World's Fair in June and would be leaving for Hong Kong the next morning, then on to various countries in Southeast Asia. Starting at 8:00 p.m., the Shanghai International Chess Association and the Xiqing Association specially selected the most formidable chess players in Shanghai, forming eleven teams arranged in a semi-circle. Dr. Euwe sat in the center, facing inward. Mr. Scherwijn (son-in-law of Mr. Tanai Pan), from Portugal, reported the moves of the opponents to Dr. Euwe in sequence, and Mr. Scherwijn moved the pieces according to Dr. Euwe's instructions. The match ended at 2:30 a.m. The results were: Xie Xiaxun and Yang Wenkai (Chinese) of team one, Mr. Ely et al. (American) of team two, Mr. Missbert et al. (Danish) of team three, Mr. Pompeii et al. (Italian) of team four, Mr. Paiche et al. (American) of team five, and Mr. Peng Taissky et al. (Dutch-Austrian) of team six all drew. Mr. Diamon and Popoff (Czech) of team seven, Mr. Polikoff et al. (Russian) of team eight, and Mr. Freeman et al. (Russian) of team nine were all completely defeated by Dr. Euwe. Mr. Tanai Pan et al. (Portuguese) of team ten and the Finland family (Finnish) of team eleven were all victorious over Dr. Euwe.

The Disaster Area Fire Insurance Association Sent Representatives to Beijing Yesterday to Petition

| Requesting the Authorities to Negotiate Compensation |

Regarding the fire insurance claims in the disaster areas, the Disaster Area Fire Insurance Compensation Promotion Association believes that the foreign merchants only recognize relief but refuse to provide compensation. Negotiations by the Social Affairs Bureau and business figures such as Yu Qiaqing for compensation have yielded little results. The representatives departed from Shanghai for Beijing yesterday morning.

Recent News from the Huashang Public Bus Company

Talks with Huang Zhongwen

Huang Zhongwen, General Manager of the Huashang Public Bus Company, made the following remarks to visitors: The Huashang Public Bus Company was established in Shanghai four years ago. Business has generally been good, but in recent years, due to the impact of the financial crisis, it has suffered significant losses. Unfortunately, it was further affected by the January 28th Incident, lending nine buses to the 19th Route Army for transportation purposes, but the compensation has not yet been received due to procedural issues. At this time of recovery, we are facing immense difficulties. We are still striving to continue, hoping to live up to the trust placed in us by the municipal government. If the Jiangwan Municipal Business Sub-Office is dissatisfied with our company's service, we would be grateful for their direct guidance and will sincerely accept it. According to the company's past operations, in 1931, the Jiangwan route had 2.4 million passengers, with an average of nine to ten buses dispatched daily. Since the resumption of operations after the war last year, over a period of seven months, we have had a total of 620,000 passengers, with an average of six to seven buses dispatched daily. Compared to the entire year of 1931, the number of passengers per bus is still 90,000 fewer. However, in the past, there were no criticisms or accusations of endangering public safety. Overloading vehicles causes damage to the machinery, as anyone familiar with the automobile industry would know. As for the service staff on the buses, the company has specific regulations to ensure their compliance. Furthermore, all employees, both senior and junior, have identification numbers. The public is welcome to report any violations of the regulations. If the Jiangwan Chamber of Commerce Sub-Office is truly working for the benefit of the people, we would be honored to receive such information. The company's service remains consistent, but in the past, when business was good, the company was favored by all parties and provided a significant number of free ride tickets each year. Due to the difficult business environment after the war, in order to conserve resources, the board of directors decided, with great reluctance, to temporarily cancel all tickets. These are the differences before and after the war. We hope this announcement is made public. The authorities may issue instructions to the company in the near future. We have no other intentions except to serve the public. If there are any shortcomings, we will improve accordingly. After Mr. Huang's statement, the visitor asked, "Regarding the municipal government's revitalization plan and the development of the city center, how is your company preparing to meet the transportation needs?" Mr. Huang replied, "The response plan has already been formulated. When the municipal government building is completed, we plan to open three new routes: (1) From Baoshan Road, via Ketiyu Road, Yinxiang Road, Songhu Road, to the new municipal building, then to Jungong Road and Wusong Town; (2) From North Sizhulu Road, East Baoxing Road, via Shuidian Road, Tiyu Road, Jiangwan Racecourse, to Jiangwan Town; (3) From Diswei Road, Qimei Road, Yinxiang Road, Jungong Road, to Shanghai University. We are actively preparing, but the capital issue is a concern. The company has recently issued new shares. If it were not for the ripple effects of the rumor-mongering, the matter would not be difficult to accomplish. The results of the share increase are also not bad. We hope for the support of all sectors to allow the local people to run the local business, so that the company's plans can be implemented on time. We have high hopes for this."

Large-Scale Counterfeit Money Operation Cracked in Datangzhen

Printing Equipment and Colored Paper Seized

Cao Lianheng Unrepentant, Specializing in Counterfeit Bills

On January 24th, Detective Feng Baishun, Detective Sun Dehui, and Detective Jin Haibo of the Huishi Police Station arrested two major suspects involved in counterfeiting, Zhou Baosheng from Shanghai and Cao Jinbao from Jiangyin, in Room 28 of the Anle Hotel on North Zhejiang Road. Ten counterfeit ten-yuan bills were found on Zhou. Based on their confession that the counterfeit bills were given to them by a Mr. He, the husband of a Mrs. He from Changzhou, a request was made to the French Concession police station to send additional detectives to No. 247 Route Lafayette to arrest Mr. He. However, he had already fled, leaving only Mrs. He at home. Fifty counterfeit five-yuan bills were found hidden in her shoes. She became flustered and, under the pretext of entering the room, took off her shoes and threw them into the toilet. The detectives initially had no intention of questioning her, but seeing her suspicious behavior, they followed her into the room, retrieved the shoes, and found the counterfeit bills, leading to her arrest. Subsequently, Chen Yushan and Chen Wangshi from Jiangbei, Zhang Rongqing from Shanghai, and Lu Wenxiang from Changzhou were also arrested in the house. Eighty-five counterfeit five-yuan bills were found hidden on Zhang. The following day, they were sent to the First Special District Local Court and ordered to be detained for investigation, as previously reported. On New Year's Eve of the old lunar calendar, the detectives again found Cai Luozhang from Changzhou and Cao Lianheng from Anhui at No. 247 Route Lafayette and in a bungalow on Fuli Road. Cao specialized in counterfeiting banknotes. His case was exposed in 1927 and he was sentenced to four years in prison by the court. After his sentence expired, he gathered accomplices to resume his old business. His counterfeiting operation was located at No. 57 Li's residence, under the address of Li Guixiang in Beishiqiao, Datangzhen, Baoshan County, and was very large in scale. On January 28th, Detective Feng and others went to the address, but Li Guixiang had already fled. All the printing equipment and colored paper were seized and transported back to Shanghai. Yesterday morning, Cai and Cao were escorted to the First Special Court and interrogated by Judge Liu Yugui. Wang Yaotang, the police station's lawyer, presented the details of the case and requested a postponement to combine the case with Zhou Baosheng and others. Detective Feng reported on the continued arrest of suspects and the seizure of equipment. Judge Liu briefly questioned Cai Luozhang and Cao Lianheng and ordered them to be detained pending a combined hearing.

Shanghai Inland Water Company to Implement New Business Regulations Today

Since the Shanghai Inland Water Company was issued a reorganization plan by the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities in 1928, it has added new-style rapid filtration ponds and changed to electric water suction machines. The equipment was improved and completed in July 1931, resulting in clean water quality and high pressure. The company also replaced large-diameter water pipes and installed water meters universally, abolishing the fixed-rate system and calculating water charges according to meter readings. By the end of 1932, all water meters for users were installed, adding up to more than two million yuan in equipment costs. Recently, because the original business regulations were no longer applicable, the company was ordered by the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities to revise them to make them perfect. The revision has now been approved by the Municipal Government and will be implemented on February 1st of this year. The internal operating procedures have also been greatly improved, and the procedures for users to apply for water supply have been expedited to benefit citizens. It is also reported that the company has a loan program to help those who are unable to afford to install water pipes. Furthermore, in areas with large numbers of common people, retail taps have been set up to sell water at low prices, so citizens of Nanshi, regardless of their social class, can enjoy clean and hygienic drinking water. These are all recent achievements of the company's efforts.

Painter Zhang Zongyu Returns from France

Arriving in Shanghai in the Next Few Days

Mr. Zhang Zongyu, after graduating from the Nanjing Art College, studied Chinese and Western painting with famous domestic painters for many years. In the spring of 1929, he went to France and in the winter, he was admitted to the French National School of Fine Arts in Paris, where he studied with the famous painter Professor Luc··EN Simon. The professor highly praised him. In the spring of 1931, he passed the French national examination. In the winter of the same year, he also studied various stage settings with Berlin, a stage painter. The painter greatly appreciated him. Now that he has completed his studies, he returned to China on the French mail ship FelixRoussel from Marseille, France, on December 30th. He is expected to arrive in Shanghai on February 3rd or 4th.

Publication of the Pure Land Five Sutras

In recent times, after Liu of Yushoutang, Guichi, meticulously engraved and printed a large number of woodblock editions of rare and ancient books, Liu of Jiayetang, Wuxing, and Li Xu of Nanling followed suit and competed with them. However, with the prevalence of lithographic and letterpress printing, the publication of woodblock books has become increasingly rare, which is regretted by general book collectors who value editions. Thereupon, Guo Shuangbai, the owner of Luzhai in Chaoyang, has entrusted Dong of Songfen Studio in Wujin to meticulously proofread, engrave, print, and bind rare and ancient books for many years. Ten kinds have already been published, which has a great style of following in the footsteps of Wu's Yue Ya, and most of them are Buddhist scriptures and rare books of exhortation to good, with clear and elegant lines, large and pleasing characters, clean and white paper, and fragrant and radiant ink. The aim is to attract the initial faith of book collectors who have not yet developed a heart and to explore Buddhist principles. It is indeed a unique and commendable effort. Not only does it surpass the two Lius, but it also shines brightly with the collection of wooden-block Buddhist classics before and after. Therefore, famous people and dignitaries, such as Duan Zhichuan, Xu Juren, Chen Zhenru, Zhu Ziqiao, Zhang Taiyan, Fu Yuanshu, Dai Jitao, and Wang Yiting, have praised it as solemn and elite, and something never before seen. It is heard that another edition of the Pure Land Five Sutras has recently been published, which has been revised by Master Yin Guang. It collects the essential sutras of the Pure Land School, such as the Amitabha Sutra, the Contemplation Sutra, the Infinite Life Sutra, the Chapter on Perfect Penetration of Mindfulness of the Buddha by the Bodhisattva Mahasthamaprapta, and the Vows of the Bodhisattva Samantabhadra, into one volume, forming a great compendium. It is a large six-opening book on cotton paper, one thick volume per set. The selling price, excluding the cost of the plates and engraving, only covers the cost of paper, ink, printing, and binding, which is two silver dollars. It is entrusted to Dong of Wujin, located in Ju Huili, Seymour Road, for consignment sales.

Reduced Price Round-Trip Tourist Tickets on Two Routes

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations have decided to add the sale of round-trip tourist tickets for the Beijing-Hangzhou first and second class express trains at Nanjing and Hangzhou stations from February 1st of this year. The fare is calculated at 75% of the original round-trip price. The validity period is ten days, and it is possible to split the journey at the Shanghai North Station midway to benefit tourists. The announcement was issued by the Transportation Department under Vehicle No. 224. All reduced-price round-trip tourist tickets for the Beijing-Hangzhou route will be implemented from February 1st.

Deceased in Fuyuanli Had Committed 15 Theft Cases

| Died of Injuries from a Fall Yesterday |

The body of a man was suddenly discovered outside No. 6 Fuyuanli, Kangding Road, Shanghai West, at about 5:00 a.m. the day before yesterday. Yao Baoshun, the street sweeper of the house, reported it to the Gordon Road Police Station, which ordered Chinese Detective Zhang Liang to investigate. A wallet was found on the deceased, containing several cards with the words "Shao Hougen, Detective No. 14, Taicang Public Security Bureau." The detective immediately sent the body to the Fielun Road Morgue for examination, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that the police station found that the deceased lived at No. 31 Jiangjiaqiao, Xiaoshadu Road, and also found in the fingerprint files that the deceased was also known as Gu Guisheng, and had committed as many as 15 theft cases in the concessions. Footprints were found on the roof of No. 4 Fuyuanli, indicating that someone had walked there. It is feared that the deceased intended to commit theft but fell accidentally. The police station sent someone to the Taicang Public Security Bureau to inquire if there was such a person, but there has been no reply yet. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, Prosecutor of the First Special District Local Court, together with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, went to the morgue to examine the body. After examining the body, they sat in court and interrogated the deceased's wife, Shao Zhangshi, who claimed to be 22 years old. On the second or third day of the lunar new year, a friend of her husband named A Si came to gamble with her husband. He came twice again on the fourth day. Then the two of them went out together and did not return. She did not know that her husband had committed crimes and said that Gu Guisheng was her husband's brother's name. Guo Jun obtained the confession and determined that Shao Hougen died of injuries to the head from a fall during his lifetime. The body was handed over to his wife, Shao Zhangshi, to take back for burial after signing a guarantee.

Tragedy After Visiting the Park with His Girlfriend

| Huang Zhengyou Commits Suicide by Poison |

Huang Zhengyou, a native of Changzhou, is 24 years old, young and handsome, and well-dressed. He visited Hongkou Park with his girlfriend the day before yesterday, talking and laughing as they walked, in a state of great happiness. Shortly after, his sister and her close friends also came to the park. They caught sight of Zhengyou talking intimately with his girlfriend, and she became extremely angry. She immediately reprimanded Huang, who did not say a word and returned home dejectedly. After his sister returned home, she complained to her parents and blamed him, and sent someone to watch him and prevent him from going out. Huang was extremely depressed at home and had attempted suicide twice without success. Last night, he secretly went out and checked into Room 13 of the Changzhou Inn on North Zhejiang Road, where he committed suicide by swallowing poison. The waiter discovered it and reported it to the Huishi Police Station, which ordered Western Police Officer No. 350 to the scene and accompanied him to the Tongren Hospital for treatment, but he died at midnight.

Meeting Records of the Bean and Rice Industry Guilds

Bean and Rice Industry: The North and South City Rice Groups of the Industry Guild held a joint meeting of all members at Cuixiutang in the city on January 31st at 2:00 PM. More than 70 people attended. The meeting proceeded as scheduled. Chairman Zhu Zixiang reported on the business transfer situation of the North and South industry in the past year. This year, the industry rules should be rectified, and submitted for discussion: (1) It was resolved that commissions should be paid in accordance with the old rules: 6% for cash payment, and 4% for clearing accounts at the end of the month. The North and South industries should abide by them uniformly. Those who violate the rules will be severely penalized after being examined by the Guild. (2) Checks should be rejected according to the rules. If a reliable customer uses a check, it must be clearly stated that it will be exchanged for a zhuang ticket immediately, with a stamp affixed, before it can be accepted. (3) Following the resolution, new measuring instruments will be used, starting tomorrow (i.e., today). The meeting adjourned after six hours.

Rice Shop Industry: The Guild has determined that new measuring instruments will be used from February 1st of this year. The capacity of the new measuring instruments is different from the old ones, and the price of rice should also be determined according to the new measuring instruments. Yesterday, the Guild convened an executive committee meeting and decided on the market price of the new measuring instruments as follows: High-grade white japonica rice: 10 yuan per dan, No. 2 white japonica rice: 9.4 yuan, No. 3 white japonica rice: 8.8 yuan, White yuan: 11 yuan per dan, High-grade indica rice: 9.2 yuan, No. 2 indica rice: 8.8 yuan, No. 3 white indica rice: 8 yuan. The industry will be notified immediately to sell according to the above market prices after using the new measuring instruments from February 1st, without any discrepancies, in order to ensure uniformity.

City News

Recent News from the Sino-Foreign Document Agency: The Sino-Foreign Document Agency, organized by Tao Shujin and others in Renle Village, Lane 124, Luban Road, has been receiving a steady stream of clients from all walks of life entrusting them to handle various documents since its opening. Recently, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs instructed the Municipal Chamber of Commerce that all newly established companies should apply for registration within the time limit stipulated in Article 5 of the Company Law, and those companies that have been established but have not yet applied for registration must be punished according to law before June 30, 1933. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce complied, and once discovered, they will be punished according to law. There are countless businesses in the city that use the words "company" or similar words, but in the past, due to unclear procedures or inconvenient transportation, there were many that had not applied for registration. Since receiving the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs' instruction transferred by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, companies that have been established but not yet registered, in order to protect their legal interests, have been entrusting the agency to complete the registration procedures. Therefore, the busiest documents for the agency these days are company registrations. It is also heard that the agency is planning to recruit several clerks due to the heavy workload. Those who believe they have the ability can go to the agency to register for an interview.

Letters to the Editor

Dear Editor: I have read a news item in your newspaper yesterday entitled "The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends a Letter to the Bureau of Public Utilities Requesting the Rectification of the Jiangwan Public Buses," in which the content is entirely fabricated and intentionally disrupts the company's business. The second point stated that "ticket inspectors, ticket sellers, and drivers are mostly rude, scold, and fight, which is commonplace" is especially unfounded. It is verified that the on-board staff and workers all have identification badges and numbers. If there is any of the above behavior, it should be noted, reported to the company, and severely dismissed. However, the Jiangwan Branch Office of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce did not specify anyone, but made indiscriminate accusations and published news in the newspaper, which is related to the reputation of our members. In addition to making separate representations, we respectfully request your newspaper to provide a correction to clarify the facts. Sincerely, The Shanghai Sixth District Public Automobile Industry Workers' Union, January 31st.

To the Editors of Shenbao: I have just read a report stating, in brief, that the Ministry of Communications has investigated the complex composition of this association and has therefore cancelled the association's registration and ordered it to merge with the Chinese Aviation Association. This association considers the merger to be another issue. As for the phrase "complex composition," not only are there no facts, but it is also completely contrary to the Ministry's intention to merge. I am specifically quoting the full text of the Ministry of Communications' instruction to clarify the truth: January 25, 1933, Instruction No. 377 of the Ministry of Communications to the China Aviation Construction Association: For your information, the construction of aviation is extremely important. At this time of national crisis, the whole country should work together and unify management. The Chinese Aviation Association, reorganized from the former China Aviation National Salvation Association, aims to gather the strength of the people of the whole country to assist the government in developing the aviation industry. This association is ordered to quickly contact it for merger in order to concentrate strength and jointly plan for progress. All the Ministry's approval for the association to register under No. 808 on August 20 of last year should be revoked immediately. Please be informed accordingly. This order, with a special letter for correction, with best wishes, China Aviation Construction Association, January 31st.

Readers' Advisory

Where is China's Problem?

| Letter from Mr. Shen Zuguang |

It goes without saying that the current Chinese political organization is hopeless! But does being hopeless mean we should just accept it? That would be underestimating the Chinese people too much. However, the Chinese people have reached this stage and are still sound asleep, so we desperately want to roll up our sleeves and do something for the country. But we think, "If you prepare for something, you will succeed. If you don't prepare, you will fail." China has been reforming for twenty-two years, and the results have always been unsatisfactory! This is because of the problem of "doing things and then seeing how they go." So our idea is, if we don't act, then so be it, but if we are going to act, how should we act for China? This is a question that must be systematically and logically studied first. We have a premise: What does it mean to be a good country? A good government? My answer is very simple: "Everyone in the country lives in peace and prosperity." If we think carefully, the country is established by people; the reason people exist is to live. The reason China has become like this is that the Chinese people cannot live; that is, they cannot live in peace and prosperity. If people cannot live in peace and prosperity, it means the political organization is not good. But how can a political organization be considered good? This is the question. For twenty-two years, China has tried all kinds of political systems, and none of them have worked. Originally, each country has its own history, human feelings, customs, and habits. Whether it is the federal republic of the United States, or the constitutional monarchy of England and Japan, the national systems of each country are different, like axes, chisels, and adzes, each with its own use. It is good to seek what suits the national conditions and harmonizes with customs, why imitate others? I have friends who are university professors and news reporters, all around thirty years old. I asked them, is a republic and democracy good for Chinese politics? Or is a constitutional monarchy good? Their opinions mostly say, regardless of which system, as long as everyone can live in peace and prosperity, a republic is fine, and a monarchy is fine. I think everyone supports a republic and democracy, simply for the sake of the two words "civil rights." Looking at it now, where are civil rights? Life and property cannot be guaranteed! And you talk about civil rights. Everyone does not recognize the monarchy, simply because the monarch has the power of life and death, according to one person's will, which is not according to the law. But from a historical perspective, the monarch's power of life and death only applies to those who are appointed and receive salaries; in fact, if those who are appointed and receive salaries are let go, they will be like Han Liu in Shandong, and the two Lius in Sichuan, fighting each other! If the monarch imposes even a death penalty on the people, it is very solemn! (Like the pre-Qing dynasty, Yu Jue went through several levels of detailed interrogation, this is what I heard from old people.) It is definitely not like now, where killing a person is not even worth a dog! What kind of world is this? If China had a constitutional monarchy, perhaps the years and current warlord battles could be seen less often? I also think, for any organization with power, whether it is big or small, I think a dictatorial system is good. Although the United States is a republic, its president is Lincoln, and Stalin of Russia, are both dictatorships. Now those great men and gentlemen, who advocate democracy, are all ambitious and using it for their own benefit. If democracy has no leader, what will it become? Once you recognize a leader, you cannot but admire heroes! My friends also have their own views on supporting a constitutional monarchy, believing that the monarch is a figurehead, and a constitution has a congress, which is better than you now having no constitution! The people cannot speak! It is always better. I also remember when Hongxian failed, Yang Du had a telegram of self-blame, he said, constitutional monarchy, initiated by Yang Du; monarch's crime, the crime lies with Yang Du. He also said, the people elect a president, for a five-year term, which is five years of chaos. Although the presidential era is not long, his words have some reason. If the current situation is not changed, revolution, revolution, will革 away the lives of the people, and the life of the country! This is truly a tearful and unspeakable situation! I don't know if you will listen to what we have to say? Maybe you will say we are turning back the clock? I think there is no absolute good or bad political system, it all depends on governance by people. Therefore, King Zhuang of Chu appointed Sun Shuao, Duke Huan of Qi used Guan Zhong, and Emperor Gaozu of Han trusted Zhang Liang and Chen Ping, and all of them achieved hegemony in the world. Therefore, Xunzi said, "Law is a tool of governance, not the source of governance being clear or turbid." This is recognizing governance by people, not recognizing rule of law. Liang Qichao wrote "The principles of 君政民政相　." He said, "My China has been spared from changing from many rulers to one ruler for two thousand years, and the country must suddenly become strong. In the past, the thirty-seven states of America, the twenty-five states of Germany, the twenty-four states of Italy, and the ninety-two feudal lords of Japan... when they were not united, those countries could not even be listed on the globe; when they were united, they each became powerful in two continents! Why? In the past, they exhausted their people in endless conflicts, cutting off their vitality, and consuming their wealth to satisfy the private desires of their rulers; uniting them into one, they avoided this difficulty, which is why one ruler can achieve a moderately prosperous society." If Liang's words are correct, then a constitutional monarchy is of course reasonable! A federal system conflicts with his argument. Sir, you are wise, please teach us.

Reply will be published tomorrow

Today, the Ministry of Education Convenes Experts to Discuss Mass Education

| Liang Shuming Arrived in Beijing from Jinan Yesterday |

Results of the Zhejiang and Shandong Joint Examinations Announced

Zhejiang: The Zhejiang Education Department organized the spring junior high school graduation joint examination for the 21st year. The test papers for the first and second districts have been separately graded. Those who pass each subject are allowed to graduate. Those who fail one or two subjects are allowed to retake each subject once. Those who fail three or more subjects or fail two subjects, should repeat the grade according to the Ministry's order. 62 graduates in the first district, 15 in the second district, those who are allowed to retake the test, a total of 216 in the two districts, and 148 failed three or more subjects. The overall average student performance and grade, as well as the school grade, should be calculated and announced after the retake test.

Shandong: (Jinan, 31st) The graduation joint examination for primary and secondary schools in the province was announced today. In terms of group scores, Provincial No. 1 and No. 8 Middle Schools are excellent. In terms of individual scores, Private Donglu Middle School is excellent. Those with an average score of 80 or above are included in the first class, with 580 people.

Aviation School Donates Salaries to Support the Righteous Army

| All are Willing to Live Frugally |

Estimated annual donation of over 5,000 yuan. The Central Aviation School's directly affiliated district party department, through its seventh standing committee meeting, resolved to request the school's headquarters to order the entire school to donate salaries monthly to support the Righteous Army. After receiving the letter, the school headquarters immediately submitted it to the school affairs meeting yesterday for discussion. All were willing to live frugally and donate salaries for a long time to support the Righteous Army. It was unanimously resolved that from January, all officers, students, and soldiers in the school with salaries below 100 yuan will donate 1% monthly, those with salaries between 101 yuan and 200 yuan will donate 2%, those between 201 yuan and 300 yuan will donate 3%, those between 301 yuan and 400 yuan will donate 4%, and those above 400 yuan will increase accordingly. It is heard that according to this ratio, the total monthly donation to the Righteous Army is estimated to be around 400 to 500 yuan, and the annual donation will reach over 5,000 yuan. The school will support the Righteous Army for a long time to help the Righteous Army resist for a long time. Their enthusiasm is commendable, and their method is good. It is hoped that all regions and institutions can actively follow suit, which can add a unique color to the future of saving the country.

The General Assembly of Faculty and Staff of Colleges and Universities in Peiping and Tientsin Decided to Send Representatives to Various Places to Contact Anti-Japanese Work

Donate 10% of Monthly Salary to Support Anti-Japanese Military Expenses

(Special dispatch from Peiping) The Federation of Faculty and Staff of National Colleges and Universities in Peiping and Tientsin convened a general assembly of all faculty and staff at 2:00 p.m. today (28th) in the auditorium of the Law School. The attendees included Wang Jixu, Qi Yilin, Ru Renhe from Peiyang Institute of Technology, Cai Peitang from the Chinese Academy, Fan Lianqing, Cheng Zhenan, Ding Weiyi, Zhao Hongrui, Liu Yuedu, Wang Wenjing, and Wang Shenming from the Sino-French University, He Jihong, Lu Aizhi, and Wu Ping from Peking University, Li Jianxun, Yang Likui, Sun Tingying, Wu Zhenghua, Liu Jiayue, He Rizhang, Deng Meiji, Fu Jiliang, and Qiu Chun from Normal University, Xu Zongwei, Wang Yonghao, Zhao Minggao, Xu Shengzu, and Wan Cheng from Pingda Institute of Technology, Huang Jigou from Pingda Medical College, Zhao Yanting and Wei Tianlin from Pingda Academy of Arts, Qi Zhongwen, Zhai Shiliang, Liu Zihui, Liu Xingyan, Fan Wenlan, Xu Zhi, and Ms. Ding Zhixin and Ms. Zhou Wenyi from Pingda Women's Liberal Arts College, Ms. Wang Wenjin, Xu Zhongbai, Yan Jingzhi, Zhang Yongsheng, Zhou Zechang, and Yuan Zhengui from Pingda Business School, Li Xuejun, Xu Pingbai, Liu Shichuan, Bao Kuang, Lu Sibo, Fan Wanfang, Shao Songnian, and Wang Wenlin from Pingda Law School, and Wang Zhuchang, Yin Liangbi, Liu Yunchou, Yu Shiyuan, Xia Shuren, Jia Chengzhang, Xiong Depu, Li Baoren, Zhou Jianzhi, Jiang Shouchun, and Guo Jiahan, 54 people in total. Before the meeting, the city party department was not notified, and police from the Public Security Bureau came out to interfere. The representative of the Teachers' Association requested instructions from the city party department by telephone. After the city party department sent representative Hu Jiachun to contact the police, the meeting was delayed until 3:30 p.m. The presidium consisted of Li Shuhua, Li Jianxun, Wang Jixu, Liu Shichuan, and He Jihong. He Jihong was elected as the chairman, and Yuan Zhengui recorded. The ceremony was performed as usual.

Reporting Items: First, Chairman He Jihong reported the significance of the meeting. Second, Standing Committee Member Cai Zengtang reported: 1. Over the past year, the Teachers' Association has been promoting educational funding for the development of university education. 2. Matters handled in terms of documents: (1) Urging the issuance of funds, (2) Refuting Minister Zhu's opinions on reorganizing education, (3) Opposing the suspension of liberal arts and law faculties in national universities and the closure of duplicate institutions, (4) Telegraphing the League of Nations to uphold justice on the Sino-Japanese issue, etc. 3. Matters handled in terms of accounting: 1. Monthly income of regular expenses is 360 yuan, 2. Temporary income is 5,000 yuan, 3. Monthly expenditure of regular expenses is 40 to 50 yuan, 4. Temporary expenditure of three southern trips for representatives is about 5,000 yuan, 5. There is a surplus of more than 1,500 yuan. Monthly income and expenditure statements have been sent to each college and university and representatives of each college and university attending the meeting. Next, Standing Committee Member Yang Likui reported on the situation of comforting the anti-Japanese soldiers. Then, the discussion of each case began.

Motions Passed: 1. How should the colleges and universities collect and donate funds to the fighting soldiers at the front? Resolution: Starting from January of this year, 10% of the total higher education funding in Peiping and Tientsin will be donated monthly, limited to two months. The association will notify each college and university to handle it accordingly. 2. How should the use of the donated funds be stipulated? Resolution: It will be handled by the Standing Committee of the Teachers' Association for review. 3. How should effective assistance work be researched? Resolution: The Standing Committee of the Teachers' Association will study it in detail, and each member will contribute their opinions to the association at any time. 4. How should representatives be elected to report to all sectors of society in domestically convenient locations and to contact assistance to the anti-Japanese work? Resolution: Passed. The Standing Committee of the Teachers' Association will decide on the number of representatives and where they should go. 6. Temporary motion: Send a letter to each college and university to add some people to participate in the Standing Committee of the Teachers' Association to study anti-Japanese work. Resolution: Passed. The Standing Committee of the Teachers' Association will decide on the number of people and how each college and university should elect them. The association will notify each college and university to handle it accordingly.

Anti-Opposition Talk: The most intense debate occurred during the discussion of Article 4, which was "How should representatives be elected to report to all sectors of society in domestically convenient locations and to contact assistance to the anti-Japanese work?" There were quite a few people who advocated not sending representatives to various places for propaganda, among whom Ms. Zhou Yuanyi, a female member, was the main figure. After Ms. Zhou spoke, the audience applauded in agreement. Later, after the eloquence of Jia Chengzhang and Liu Shichuan, when the vote was taken, it passed the "Motion to elect representatives to go to domestically convenient locations, report to all sectors of society, and contact assistance to the anti-Japanese work." After the meeting adjourned, Ms. Zhou had the following conversation with the reporter: "The members attending today's meeting are less than one-tenth of the total membership. There are more than a thousand members in total. It is quite illegal for a meeting with a small number of attendees to pass the motion to elect representatives to go to domestically convenient locations, report to all sectors of society, and contact assistance to the anti-Japanese work. We must awaken the people for the anti-Japanese movement, but it is superfluous for the Teachers' Association to send representatives to domestically convenient locations to publicize to all sectors of society. In areas with convenient transportation, there are newspapers to read, and almost everyone knows the necessity of resisting Japan. Moreover, the people in the transportation locations are already engaged in the anti-Japanese movement. Why does our association need to send representatives to publicize? As for reporting the situation on the front line, it is also inappropriate, because the situation on the front line is constantly changing. Can the Teachers' Association representatives' one-time inspection of the situation on the front line be used as permanent reporting material? At present, our association's funds are not sufficient, so it must spend a lot of money to provide travel expenses for the representatives. It is agreed in principle that the faculty and staff of various colleges and universities will donate 20% of their two-month salaries to the anti-Japanese soldiers at the front, but I absolutely oppose using a portion of this money for travel expenses for the representatives. It is okay for the faculty and staff of various colleges and universities to donate a portion of their hard-earned salaries to the anti-Japanese soldiers, but it is not okay to use this money to subsidize the travel expenses of the representatives. In fact, sending letters and telegrams can already achieve the purpose of publicity, and there is no need to waste public funds and be used as travel expenses for a few people."

Letter to Various Colleges and Universities: Dear Sir, The General Assembly of Faculty and Staff of National Colleges and Universities in Peiping and Tientsin resolved today that the colleges and universities should donate funds to the fighting soldiers at the front for the purpose of purchasing heavy trucks and other military supplies. 10% of the amount of higher education funding will be deducted monthly for a period of two months. Please retain the donations that have already been deducted from the funding items of the colleges and universities in January. We will send another letter to request payment when needed. Accordingly, we send this letter and ask you to handle it accordingly. Sincerely, Peiping and Tientsin National Colleges and Universities Faculty and Staff Federation, 28th. (Sent on the 28th)

Notify this museum for liaison and discussion. Items for discussion: 1. Submitting a request to the central government and sending a letter to the Guangdong Provincial Government and Shanghai Municipal Government to subsidize the museum's funding for public transportation. Resolved and passed. 2. The museum's emblem was resolved to add the two words "Sun Yat-sen" to the emblem of the Kuomintang. The meeting adjourned at 4:30 p.m. It was also heard that regarding the matter of requesting funding from the central government, Li Dachao will go to Beijing to negotiate, and request the Guangdong Provincial Government to subsidize 10,000 yuan per month, and ask Hu Hanmin to contact him nearby.

The Municipal Education Bureau Reviews the Academic Status Law for Transferred Students from Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang

The Municipal Education Bureau of this city, in order to review the academic status of transferred students from Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang, specially issued an order to the schools in this city: In accordance with the regulations, the new students and transfer students reported by the middle schools in this city are reviewed by the bureau after the certificate documents are verified, so as to ensure accuracy and avoid luck. Since the "September 18th Incident" occurred, all schools in the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang have been reduced to war zones. Whether the academic status of the students transferred to the middle schools in this city is reliable is impossible to verify before the "Northeast China Incident" is resolved. In order to prevent fraud, the Bureau formulated the "Measures for Reviewing the Academic Status of Transferred Students from Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang", which was approved by the 251st Bureau Affairs Meeting. Hereby, a copy of the measures is sent to the school. In the future, all transferred students from the three northeastern provinces should submit the entrance examination papers or other documents submitted by the student to the bureau for review, in addition to the certificate documents from the original school. You are hereby notified. This order.

The Work of the Vocational Guidance Institute in the Past Year

Qualified Registrants are Mostly Specialized Talents

4,000 People Entrusted to Make Introductions, More Than 400 People Succeeded

The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Institute of the China Vocational Education Society has been established for more than five years since its establishment in September 1927. The following is a statistical summary of various tasks in the past year:

Various Talks: Vocational talks 7,179 people, further education talks 1,549 people, personnel talks (including legal, health, marriage, etc.) 350 people, totaling 9,078 people. According to the above statistics, the number of people who received the above talks at the institute in one year reached more than 9,000, an average of 25 people per day. Most of those who gave vocational talks were asking for vocational introductions.

Talent Registration: 917 graduates from domestic and foreign universities, 708 graduates from specialized schools, 668 graduates from normal schools, 755 graduates from secondary vocational schools, 733 graduates from secondary schools, 550 students who have completed secondary schools, and 321 others, totaling 4,652 people. According to the proportion of the above registrants, the number of specialized talents with special skills who graduated from domestic and foreign universities is the largest, and the number of students who have completed secondary schools and are unable to continue their studies is small. Men account for 88.4%, and women account for 11.6%. Among them, the most successful introductions are in education, followed by commerce, industry, and public works. The positions are mostly teachers, accountants, clerks, and trainees, followed by engineers, technicians, and ticket sellers.

Vocational Introduction: 127 school teachers, 144 institution staff (including accountants, clerks, and technicians), 17 factory staff apprentices, 83 store staff trainees, 40 ticket sellers, and 24 others, totaling 435 people. According to the above statistics, more than 4,000 people have entrusted the introduction of occupations in one year, and more than 400 people have succeeded, with a ratio of one to ten.

Other Guidance: 93 cases of acting as a planner, 93 cases of acting as an investigator, 9 cases of acting as a talent examiner, 264 cases of acting as a talent scout. According to the above statistics, on average, there are two cases of acting as a planner and investigator each week, and on average, there is more than one case of acting as a talent scout each day. Talent examination is a temporary nature, and there are 69 people for legal guidance, 124 people for health guidance, 9 service guidance (opening service talk meetings), 9 vocational speeches. When holding service talk meetings, leaders and experts of various industries are invited to give speeches. Each time, 100 to 200 people attend. This talk meeting and speech are generally classified as vocational training. More than 1,000 people receive training each year.

Theory and Practice of Vocational Education Reprinted

"Theory and Practice of Vocational Education," compiled and published by the China Vocational Education Society, is a comprehensive special book on vocational education in the country. Its content is insightful, encompassing theories of vocational education in all aspects and practical management methods. Shortly after its publication, letters requesting purchases have been received from dozens of provincial education departments, over two hundred local education bureaus, over three hundred local libraries, and over five hundred normal schools and vocational schools. In addition, over ten institutions plan to adopt it as a textbook for the next semester, including the Education College of Central University, the Education Department of Guanghua University, and the Education College of Daxia University. The first edition is now sold out. Requests for purchase continue to arrive from various places. The Society is making efforts to expedite printing and will be able to publish it soon. The price remains the same (paperback: 1.3 yuan, hardcover: 1.6 yuan). Publisher: China Vocational Education Society, Hualong Road, Shanghai. General distributor: Shanghai Life Bookstore. Distributors are located in Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Beiping, Tianjin, Guangzhou, Hangzhou, and Hankou.

=Australian Sixteen-Year-Old Youth=

=Defeats Tennis King Vines=

(Sydney, 30th) Crawford retained the Australian Open Tennis Championship, defeating Granshee in the final, a member of the American touring tennis team to Australia. The score was 2-6, 7-5, 6-2, 6-2.

Stars Gather

In addition, this Australian Open Championship has gathered all the world's first-class players. The top ten players, such as Vines, Allison, Van Ryn, etc., are all representatives of the American Davis Cup. However, they were all eliminated one by one. As a result, Crawford won.

The Failure of the Tennis King

The most surprising news in the entire competition was the failure of the world tennis king, Vines, to the Australian sixteen-year-old McGrath. The two met in the semi-final, and Mai won in four sets, 6-2, 2-6, 7-5, 8-6. It shows that Fan also tried his best to deal with it. Mai has created a great career in a short tennis life.

Doubles Championship

The doubles championship was won by the American team, Vines and Granshee. In the final, they defeated the Australian team, Crawford and Moon, with a score of 6-4, 10-8, 6-2.

Commercial News

Rumors of US Issuing Paper Money

Gold Price Drops Slightly by 3 Liang and 3 Qian

Lingering Around 780 Liang All Day

City Overview

After a slight increase the day before yesterday, the market saw a decline yesterday. Although it rose by 3 liang the day before yesterday, it was still far from the downward trend in the silver market during the four-day closure. Therefore, those who took positions the day before yesterday immediately expected the silver market to rise. Yesterday's telegrams showed that London large bars, both near-term and far-term, rose by 125, and both the British-American and American-British exchange rates rose by more than half a point. The New York silver price increased by 375. The far-term silver price on the Metal Exchange rose by 5 to 40 points. Although American cotton fell by more than 10 pounds, bank private telegrams showed an increase of 375. Therefore, the gold market opened slightly lower, at 784.5 liang, with very good sentiment, pushing it to 786 liang. However, the exchange rate remained strong. Miscellaneous Grains Stable Without Progress

Yesterday, the market for miscellaneous grains was stable. Dingjiazhou yellow soybeans were traded for 1,000 bags. Dasheng Daily Sutra

(1) Opening of the White Willow

"Business Sutra" is originally a kind of experience in doing business, which can also be said to be a knack. This knack is nothing more than saying how to make this business successful and how to sell this batch of goods. In order to achieve this goal, the methods, means, language, jokes, etc. used are generally called "Business Sutra".

The purpose of this column continuing these three words is to introduce the "Business Sutra" used in doing business to the readers of this newspaper. The reason is that general consumers have a similar feeling, that is, it is easy to use things but difficult to buy things. The difficulty lies in the fact that there are so many commodities related to people's daily life, and it is not easy to know how to buy these commodities. That is, this column cannot solve them one by one, but if the articles related to daily clothing, food, etc. can be explained, it is not without some ways to obtain some insights in the consumer aspect, which can be used as a reference when buying things. Then, the opening of this style may not be without some convenience to consumers.

However, there are various kinds of commodities, which cannot be generalized. Readers still need to draw inferences from one instance, especially what can be promoted by pen and ink is only a general outline. Inevitably, there are shortcomings. If you want to expand and correct it, I hope to get the support of the readers. As for the manuscripts in this column, in addition to specially invited contributions from people in various industries, contributions are still welcome. (1) Contributions should take a single commodity as a descriptive unit, regardless of literary or vernacular language, each should be about 300 to 400 words; (2) Once a contribution is published, it will be paid handsomely, but the copyright belongs to this newspaper; (3) If there are multiple submissions of the same manuscript or plagiarism, once discovered and verified, no payment will be made; (4) The submitted items will be disclosed by this newspaper at any time, and the time limit cannot be specified. Whether it is published or not, it will not be returned; (5) Each manuscript must separately state the real name, correspondence address, and seal or signature style; (6) If there are any questions about the submitted manuscript, the contributor shall be invited to the museum for face-to-face consultation and shall not refuse.

Five cars of Lianzhu soybeans were purchased by merchants in the inner city and Guangdong, but the factories remained unmoved. 300 bags of Pudong Duzhu soybeans were imported into the street. The future of the soybean market is that the sales are ordinary, and cities such as Dalian are also weakening, so it is easy to fall in Shanghai but difficult to rise. Mung beans are still only consumed by small Luzon and Hong Kong, with a total of more than 130 bags of Guandian large-grain vegetable mung beans and 200 bags of Ming mung beans being traded. Jiangbei mung beans were purchased by Xiamen merchants. 200 bags of long beans were taken by Little Luzon. Silk and Tea

Tea House Policies Remain Unchanged

However, tens of thousands of yuan have been released along the Sui'an Road

There are no less than 20 local tea houses in this port that deal with Ping Shui tea. They are the hub of the tea industry in terms of financial receipts and disbursements and business dealings. Due to the high prices of inland tea last year, the sale of foreign green and black tea in Shanghai had fallen without rising, causing most tea houses to suffer slight losses. Since the final accounts were closed, Hong Yuancheng, Yuan Fengrun, Zhongxinchang, Yong Shengchang, Yong Xinglong, Sheng Changsheng, Gong Shengyong, etc. have successively determined this year's business policy, which is generally unchanged. However, many tea houses along Sui'an Road are paying attention. It is heard that tens of thousands of yuan have been released one after another.

The factory's small bag of ice No. 1 opened at 17 taels and 8 qian, and No. 2 at 17 taels and 7 qian.

Chao Merchants' Rules Have Been Resolved

The Chao merchants and the sugar industry had changes in their rules due to the issue of changing the market scale. Yesterday, the two parties reached a decision after consultation at the old public hall in the South City, which will be implemented as long as the two parties notify their peers today. The key points of the decision are recorded as follows: (1) Silver term: The deadline is 10 days from the date the transaction is written on the ticket; (2) Warehouse rent: Starts one month later; (3) The shipment must be cleared within three months; (4) Fire insurance is limited to three months (paid by the house); (5) When the silver term expires, the bank will first pay the house with the goods and silver, and then the house will send the bill of lading to the bank; (6) The packaging skin is stipulated to be 2 jin and 12 taels per bag (market scale).

Last Year's Sugar Industry Profit Report

In the 21st year, the sugar industry was affected by the Shanghai war in the first half of the year, and the business was inevitably affected. Therefore, the result was a feeling of mixed joys and sorrows. A total of 15 companies made profits, one was reorganized, and one was liquidated.
