Oil Market

A Review of Last Year's Oil and Hemp Business

The tung oil and ramie industry has gradually declined in the past four or five years, and even more so last year. The business has not increased compared to the previous year. The reasons are as follows: 20 years ago, old prefectures such as Jinhua, Quzhou, Wenzhou, Yanzhou, etc. in Zhejiang Province and counties in the upper reaches of Hangzhou Prefecture all developed barren mountains and planted tung trees. In the past ten years, the production volume has increased sharply. The area where Hantong was sold has become a production area. Oil and hemp houses in this port used to purchase from Hankou and sell to inland cities and towns in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Zhejiang production has accumulated and is cheaper than Han production. The business in this port has gradually been occupied by Zhejiang production. Although Zhejiang sales have been cut off, local provinces can still be maintained. Zhejiang tung oil sales to Jiangsu Province require a tax of 7 jiao and 2 fen per load. After the tax cards were abolished, the obstacles were removed, and Zhejiang tung oil sales to Jiangsu were unobstructed. Shanghai used to rely on foreign customs as a talisman, but now there is nothing to rely on to resell inland. The business opportunity is on the verge of extinction. This white tung oil is affected by the sharp increase in Zhejiang production and the abolition of tax. The main business of Hantong oil has been completely plundered. However, Hongjiang tung oil may be able to maintain a part of it. However, the history of Hongtong oil shows that before the establishment of tax cards, the market was concentrated in Suzhou. Later, due to the difficulty of transportation for merchants due to the establishment of numerous tax cards in the interior, this port could rely on foreign customs to transport and resell. The market has gradually shifted to Shanghai for decades. After the abolition of the tax, the business of Hongjiang tung oil in Suzhou is gradually booming, and it is expected to restore the state before the establishment of tax cards decades ago. Since the heavy tax has been lifted, there is no obstacle to loading and unloading, and Suzhou is located in the center of Zhejiang Province's Hangzhou, Jiaxing, and Huzhou and Jiangsu Province's Suzhou, Songjiang, and Changzhou, with traffic in all directions, which is far more convenient than Shanghai's remote coastal location. Due to the guidance of the situation, there should be a new trend. Therefore, the tung oil industry in this port has come to an end. This is also a drastic change in the market. Last year's business in the oil and hemp industry in this port was suspended in the first half of the year due to the war. Although it can be operated in the second half of the year, the scope of business is limited to one corner due to the above-mentioned various influences. The state of decline has reached the extreme. If no other attempts are made, it will be eliminated. It is hoped that those engaged in this business will seek new paths to find a way out. As for those who have made profits among the various houses, they are those who also operate hemp, so hemp can still make profits last year. If you specialize in tung oil, it is difficult to get a surplus.

Spring and Autumn

Shanghai Idle Talk

— Zhongxian

Beauty and Ugliness

"Above are the heavens, below are Suzhou and Hangzhou." This is a compliment to the Jiangnan region that has been passed down for thousands of years. Today, the heavenly status of Suzhou and Hangzhou has been usurped by Shanghai. Although Suzhou and Hangzhou have natural scenery, they ultimately cannot match the artificial beauty of Shanghai.

Everything in Suzhou and Hangzhou is fashionable because it is Shanghaied. Shanghai people, however, consider Westernization to be fashionable and would never deign to imitate the things of the people of Suzhou and Hangzhou. The people of Suzhou and Hangzhou are influenced by Shanghai life, and they never tire of living in Shanghai as gentlemen of leisure. Shanghai people, if they happen to go to Suzhou and Hangzhou for a day or two, will feel inconvenienced in their lives. Apart from the real mountains and real rivers, everything else is not as beautiful as in Shanghai!

Shanghai is truly a beautiful place! Especially Shanghai at night. People are intoxicated by the red lights. Looking up at the tall Western-style buildings of more than ten stories, they will feel the insignificance of their own bodies. On Jing'an Temple Road, Xiafei Road, and other places, there are many mansions of the wealthy. From among the towering pavilions and lush bamboo forests, strains of delicate music can be heard. From afar, one can see one or two fashionable girls either appearing or disappearing inside. They truly seem like immortals. The poor scholars, upon seeing them, will have all sorts of reveries in their hearts.

However, in Shanghai, there are many people who live in the "cracks." If we do not have the eyes to see through things, we will not be able to see their cramped state. It is very common for seven or eight families to live in a one-story or two-story house. Of course, the upstairs and downstairs are full of beds, and in the space between the floor and the ceiling, attics can be built to live in. Are these people not living in the cracks of the houses? How can you see their lives as you walk on the wide roads?

Shanghai is like a white porcelain manure pipe, with a shiny exterior, as beautiful as white jade. If the pipe is broken, the yellow and white matter inside will be revealed, making it look incomparably ugly!

In the waiting room of a hospital specializing in venereal diseases, a beautiful girl is sitting. She is dressed very beautifully, and there are absolutely no blemishes on her face. After a short while, the doctor asks her to take off her clothes, and one can see that her whole body is covered with spots, filled with syphilitic sores. The beauty and ugliness of Shanghai is also similar to that of this young lady. To paint the face!"

I laughed. In my heart, I thought... In the snowy mountains of the north, the blood of soldiers is still flowing, as red as rouge. It would be very good to use it as cosmetics for Chinese girls!

Women's Red Satin Trousers

— Yan Bōguāng

In January 1933, several fashionable girls, competing to show off their beauty, permed their hair into curly waves to beautify their beautiful hair, weaved fine eyebrows, had lightning-like lively eyes, cherry-like vermilion lips, qipaos more than four feet long, red satin trousers with embroidered edges, and high-heeled leather shoes with black lacquer flowers... She walked with winding artistic steps, entering and exiting major theaters and movie theaters.

Can her outfit save the country? Yes, she learned the alluring style of a star in several extremely famous Chinese films, and she also learned the heroic spirit of Mulan joining the army. She was not seen carrying a gun, nor was she seen going out to the pass to kill thieves. No, she was saving the country with fashion.

The gorgeous red trousers seduced the pursuit of young men in Western suits, who were intoxicated in her warm embrace, as if a servant could not leave his nanny. A shallow smile and a light frown, how happy he was to see. He praised her beautiful hair, saying it was like a

Indulgent and Base

— Páng Zǐsū

It seems that twenty years ago, the Japanese used the four words "indulgent and base" to describe Chinese students studying in Japan. At that time, Chinese students thought this was a great humiliation, so they were very indignant.

However, what about today, twenty-two years later? Heh... Aren't they still inheriting this old family business of "indulgent and base"?

Nothing can be believed without evidence, so let's look at the facts...

People walking on the road always like to throng in the middle of the road, as if they are preparing to fight motorcycles to the death.

Buying tickets at the train station, watching plays in the theater, getting on and off the tram, they are always impolite to each other. Those who come later want to be first, and those who arrive first fall behind.

In restaurants, it is necessary to play drinking games to be considered enjoyable, and it is necessary to have a mess of dishes and plates to be considered happy.

Playing cards and singing operas in hotels all night long is common practice. If you can't fall asleep and try to persuade them to be quiet, not only will they not apologize, but they may even say that you are interfering with their freedom.

Everywhere on the streets, you can see fights, and everywhere in the alleys, you can hear scolding.

At random, it is enough to expose all the bad habits of China, such as not keeping order, not respecting the freedom of others, and other inferior characteristics. Friends! Stop inheriting this "indulgent and base" family business!

Hometown

— Hú Tīwéi

"What time is it now?"

Hongye heard her mother say that sick people are most afraid of asking about the time, and immediately sensed that the illness was not good,

"Three twenty-five."

"Go get a pen and paper!"

Hongye didn't understand what it was for, and didn't dare to ask. She held the pen and looked at her father, and at the same time felt the need to notify her mother and brothers to get up.

Father still closed his eyes... "I thought of two elegies myself. You write them down for me, "The setting sun knows, the bright moon returns to the truth." After I die, Elder Fang from S Village, who has been a family friend for three generations, will definitely come to offer condolences. You can ask Fang Elder to write them and hang them on my spirit."

Hongye finished listening to his father, teardrops already soaked half of the letter paper. She quickly called her mother and brothers up, and one by one they quietly entered the room to sit and watch. After a while, it dawned, and her mother told Hongye to go to sleep, but Hongye didn't want to. She watched for another two hours, and her father slept soundly. Hongye felt that she couldn't hold on any longer, so she left the room and went to bed. In her mind, there were only the eight words "The setting sun knows, the bright moon returns to the truth," surging like a raging tide, and she didn't know if it was sweat or tears, soaking the pillow.

She didn't know how long she was in a daze when Hongye's brother came to call her, saying that father was not well. Hongye rushed into the room, her mother's face covered with tears, holding her father's hand...

"Hongye, father's hands are cold, call out!"

Hongye hugged her father's white-haired head, attached it to his ear, and her tears that never dried dripped on her father's haggard, emaciated cheeks...

"Dad... Dad..."

Poor father, no matter how loudly Hongye shouted, he would not open his last line of sight of his eyes, he couldn't hear! He couldn't see!

Hometown, a hometown six hundred li away! Every year on this most painful and memorable day, Hongye always rushes back to his father's grave and kowtows respectfully. During this short journey, the special express train swallowing white coal and spitting out black smoke, the small hotels where the wealthy insects stay, the C River with sandy sails and a crescent moon, the long-distance bus that goes up to the heavens and down to the underworld, and, of course, the green mountains, the precarious city walls, the skillful wine jar mountain, the stone archway praising chastity, the mosquitoes chirping and seeking each other, and everything else! Of course, there is also a loving mother, friendly brothers, all safe and sound every year. Only those most touching emaciated cheeks, the white-haired forehead, the two chubby feet in the black leather slippers, are never seen again! (The End)

The annual excitement will, as usual, cause excitement and joy for the tired villagers.

Pulling up the collar of his overcoat, burying his felt hat on his head, he turned to this temple fair. The north wind was blowing so hard that the bald trees were roaring loudly. The tall trees stood tall, with not a single leaf left. The branches trembled slightly, and the residual grass on the wild ground swelled into yellow waves. I stood in this wave, listening to the wind, and I felt lonely and cold. There was a little jealousy of those who were gambling and burning incense.

Broken, the sound of the wind was like the tide, the cloud feet dragged lower, and it was snowing. Powder-like, catkin-like, falling flower-like, the space was filled with these white demons, point by point. He immediately thought of Emperor Qianlong of the Qing Dynasty's poem about snow...

"One piece, two pieces, three or four pieces, five pieces, six pieces, seven or eight pieces, ninety-one hundred pieces, thousands of pieces..." It is truly a good poem that expresses the feeling of being in the scene. It has the leisurely mood of watching the snow begin to fly, and such a happy and cheerful mood. Mr. Ji Xiaolan thought he was very clever and ended with the last sentence... "Flying into the pear blossoms and disappearing." In fact, there is not much fun to be felt. It is only to match the so-called seven-character quatrain passed down from ancient times, which must have only twenty-eight characters.

I also chanted the Emperor's good poem and returned home step by step. I was covered in snow.

It just so happened that my nephew was catching snowflakes in the yard, freezing his fingers red as he carried them into bottles, jars, and paper bags... As soon as he saw me coming, he ran to me with a smile and said...

"Uncle, the heavens are dropping so much snow cream, but female poet saint, her eyes were like movie star Greta Garbo's. ...He asked her why she was wearing dazzling red trousers? She said... "The decline of Chinese silk is all because of people like you who love to wear Western suits. All you know is to wear beautiful Western suits and chase girls. If everyone in the country is like you, how can the country not perish? I wear red trousers to promote silk and save the country, not to charm people." He realized the truth and from then on did not use foreign goods, did not wear Western clothes, and made a determined decision to save the country. Whose credit is this?

Novel

Intoxicated

— Lan Guang

This happened half a year ago.

A tranquil atmosphere enveloped the hospital ward. A ghastly blue electric light emanated from within the ward, passing through the air vents above the doorframe. It took the form of a slanting rectangle on the stairs leading to the third floor, suddenly manifesting as an angel at the top of the stairs. She was barefoot, wearing snow-white soft-soled shoes. Her little feet, clad in snow-white socks, moved beneath the long slit of her cheongsam. She wore a silver coat—a nurse's outer garment. Her two rosy and plump cheeks bore shallow dimples, appearing even more beautiful in the pale blue light. Her wavy hair was covered by a white cap with a red cross, all possessing a charming allure.

She lightly tiptoed through the side door and walked to the patient's bedside. The patient, afflicted with typhoid fever, was struggling as if fighting death itself, constantly flailing his limbs. His eyes stared unblinkingly at the feeble light, anticipating annihilation along with the light. She gently tucked the woolen blanket around him and slowly walked away from the bed towards the stairs.

In a corner of the staircase, she seemed lost in thought. The sound of leather shoes suddenly vibrated in her ears. It was him, coming from the pharmacy, holding the patient's name tag in his hand, along with a bottle of mud-like medicine. His eyes looked up at her feet, unconsciously exerting force to lift his foot and step upward.

With about three steps left, a chaotic sound of footsteps arose behind him, followed by a chorus of voices shouting:

"Make way, make way, a patient is coming!"

It was a patient being carried up from the saline room, constantly shouting: "Want watermelon, iced jelly, sour... plum syrup!" He hurriedly moved toward the corner, but she was too late to dodge. Thus, his chest pressed tightly against her chest. He enjoyed a fleeting moment of fortune. A blush of rose-colored clouds appeared on her face, and she hastily turned towards the corner of the wall. He bent down to pick up the scattered prescription paper, now stained with shoe prints. He slowly walked into his office, sat in the chair, and as he picked up his pen, his mind was filled with this memory... silver-white coat, wavy hair, delicate and beautiful face, especially the soft and warm chest... he was intoxicated. The pen slipped from his hand, rolled off the desk, and the nib pierced into a crack in the board, swaying.

Sleepless Night

Night, quietly, silence occupied the land. Old Man Sandman forgot about me, and I still opened my eyes wide, staring at the outlines in the darkness. "Why can't I fall asleep yet?" I was annoyed, turned over, and counted one, two, three… but still did not see Old Man Sandman's arrival.

It seemed that falling asleep was impossible, so I had to open my eyes wide again and stare into the darkness. The sharp barking of dogs in the distance, like the howling of wolves in the deep mountains, made my heart tremble!

Disordered thoughts surged into my mind like a tide.

Thinking and thinking, my heart gradually became irritable, so I decided not to think, but more thoughts surged in, as if saying fiercely: "Humph, see if you can escape my control."

I muttered: "Heavens, is even a sound sleep at night not allowed after working hard all day?"

The small clock on the table chimed twelve times.

"Ah, it's twelve o'clock. Sleep! I have to get up at six o'clock tomorrow. If I sleep late, I won't have any energy to work!" I said to myself.

However, the thoughts were like wild horses, running even wilder. I thought of the red-cheeked girl I saw on the street during the day, smiling lightly, of the supervisor's devilish face, of the cotton robe still in the pawnshop, of the bandit's慷慨激昂 before execution, of the woman's snow-white feet, of…

The small clock on the table struck one, then two, then three. My thoughts were as chaotic as tangled silk threads. Dragging on and on, I didn't know how much time had passed. I heard it strike four, then five. What to do? Waiting and waiting, time seemed to pass even slower, and the disordered thoughts had also fled. I just stared blankly at the window, which was tinged with a faint light. The faint light slowly increased, finally reaching the dawn. Before long, the clock struck six, so I reluctantly struggled to get up, my body exhausted, and sighed softly... "Alas, this night!"

Free Talk

The Melting of Snow

— Xu Jie

"Snowfall is not as cold as snow remaining," this is what experience tells us.

However, this year's weather is very different from usual. Normally, after it snows in our Jiangnan weather, it wouldn't melt, nor would it accumulate. So when the snow melts, although it is cold, it is also cold in a refreshing way. But this year, the snow falls and falls, but refuses to melt at all. It seems that the world will be permanently locked down in white like this; and we humans, it seems, will right away have the hopes of a frozen crucian carp in the mud, to be frozen alive in the ice of the air. Ah! If it goes on like this, what kind of world will it be!

A few days ago, because there were still people making fires for warmth during the day, some people needed to cook, and even some people were talking and breathing, the eaves of our houses dripped with melting ice water. No matter how small this ice water was, to us, it also felt like a recovery of a lot of vitality and new hope.

We know very well that spring is coming, but watching the world freeze like this day after day, freezing our bodies and souls in severe ice and snow, those days are not easy to live through. Be patient, yes, patience is indeed our Chinese people's golden rule of conduct, but in this situation, in fact, even a moment, even a minute or a second, we can't bear it!

Have you ever seen colored glass rods and glass balls used to weigh down books or paper? Have you ever seen goldfish frozen in those glass balls? Have you ever seen two swallows with diagonally cut tails frozen in those glass rods? Yes, the way our souls are frozen is somewhat similar.

However, you may still be able to imagine one ten-thousandth of this situation, because it's just for fun, it's just a work of art made of lifeless special materials; you won't place any sympathy on the goldfish with its eyes wide open, ultimately unable to move, or on the pair of swallows with their clipped tails, ultimately unable to fly away, and worry about those lifeless things.

There's no way, let me give you another example! However, I don't know if you ever played the game of raising small fish when you were children? But for me, I have had such an experience.

In May or June, I caught many small fish and shrimp in a small stream. Because they were lively and cute, I raised them in a small tank at home. I was very afraid they would be uncomfortable with me, so I put a lot of green algae in it, and I let them hide in the rock caves of the artificial mountain and swim and play under the shade of the pine-like algae. I served them with rice grains or wheat flour every day. As soon as I sprinkled a few rice grains into the tank, they would recognize that food had arrived from the slight shattering sound on the surface of the water, and immediately run out from the rock cave or under the algae to eat. I almost had a spiritual connection with them, almost regarding them as a part of my life.

However, all the way to this year's cold winter, one night, a northwest wind suddenly arose in the air, and all the water turned completely into solid. Of course, inevitably, my small fish tank, the small fish tank that entrusted a part of my spirit, was also frozen from the root up. The next morning, when I hurried to see those little fish in the cold wind, ah, what a heartbreaking thing, they were all frozen in the whole block of ice, along with the rocks, aquatic plants, all frozen together. Oh, what a heartbreaking thing! (To be continued)

New Year's New Dreams

— Yang Qiu

The "new" "1932" has passed, and the "old" "Republic of China Year 21" has also passed. Naturally, no one is satisfied with the past year, so at the beginning of this new year, everyone is making new and satisfying dreams. This, we can clearly see from the spring couplets posted in front of the High Street Gate, such as "Business prospers and reaches the four seas, wealth flourishes and reaches the three rivers," etc., and the auspicious words posted in the study, such as "May the pen flourish in the new year, may great fortune and profit come," etc.

However, "business prospers, wealth flourishes," and "may the pen flourish in the new year, may great fortune and profit come" are ultimately just "dreams of getting promoted and becoming wealthy" centered on the individual. Moreover, such "dreams" seem to be just "I hope so," and have not clearly shown the meaning of "struggle."

The times have, after all, shattered the illusion of "getting promoted and becoming wealthy" centered on the "individual." You only see, although there are still people dreaming of "prosperous business" or "auspicious profits" at the beginning of this year, smart people have already been taught to be obedient by the times. They have already understood the meaning of "group," and even more understand the meaning of "our group" and "their group." They know that now it can't just be "I hope so," but should be "must be so," which means that now it is "necessary to struggle," not "individual against individual" struggle, but "our group against their group" struggle. Therefore, at the beginning of this year, the call for "National Goods Year" and "Suppressing Communists Year" arose one after another.

What is the meaning of "National Goods Year" and "Suppressing Communists Year"? This means that "personal dreams" have been transformed into "group and group confrontation." Smart people are urgently hoping to be dragged out of the black tide of "panic" and "turmoil" in 1933.

Will this hope be shattered? 1933 probably won't fail to answer us.

About "Rejecting Geniuses"

— Cheng Yunping

Qifan Jun previously published an article "Rejecting Geniuses" in this newspaper's Free Talk, and later Huang Zhongxi Jun raised a question in the Readers' Advisory column. Originally, the columnist in the Readers' Advisory column already had a very good answer, so I don't need to say anything more, but I still have a few words I want to say.

The largest number of people in our society are mediocre people, ordinary people. Qifan Jun's words are completely correct. Even if there are geniuses, they are only a very small number, and these people are in society. In the past, too much emphasis was placed on "genius," so geniuses became "people above people," forming a social stratum that dominated mediocre people, and thus all kinds of deception, cruelty, and tyranny arose. This kind of genius should naturally be rejected.

We have a saying that goes "Eat the bitterest of bitterness, and you can become a person above people." These so-called "people above people" are undoubtedly the ruling class. Chinese history is so long, a large part of it is the monarchical era. Feudal ideology is really deeply rooted in the minds of the people. In order to become a "person above people," they do not hesitate to lose face, abandon personality, and drill around like dogs. Once they are successful, if they do not put on a full airs, it is not enough to show their "human tool"; if they are unsuccessful, they will make a mess, and if they are no longer useful, they will become decadent, degenerate, and romantic. We can say… Chinese politics, everything, is so chaotic, this is a big problem!

The evolution of society is not entirely due to the credit of geniuses. Genius is by no means a super-class thing. I fundamentally do not recognize the existence of the individual. The individual in the entire society is like a cell in our body. The strength of one cell is not enough to make the individual healthy. The strength of all the cells is what can make the whole body strong. The relationship between people and society is roughly the same. Social evolution is not the power of a mediocre person, nor is it the power of a genius. I don't know if there are still people who doubt it?

But geniuses cannot be completely written off. The so-called genius, simply put, means that one's intelligence and talent are one level higher than the average person. It is a pity that many geniuses, because they have this level of higher intelligence and talent, want to deceive and exploit the mediocre masses in order to form their "person above people" position. Let our Mr. Qifan call out "rejection" to everyone! If geniuses are willing to join the mediocre masses and help the mediocre masses, then we have no choice but to welcome geniuses.

I understand Qifan Jun's original intention in writing "Rejecting Geniuses." He has indeed seen the symptoms of political chaos and social inequality. It is only a pity that, as the columnist in the Readers' Advisory column said, he did not separate "genius" from "person above people." However, I have already said… "Genius" becoming a "person above people" is very easy.

In conclusion, I dare to say this… if geniuses do not stand on our heads, we can welcome geniuses, otherwise, we must reject them. This society is fundamentally a society of mediocre people.

The Song of the Petrel

— Gorky, translated by Yi Xian

The petrel is a small seabird in the temperate zone with very long wings and black and white plumage. It is said that this seabird often appears before storms, so it is also called Stormy Petrel.

This poem is one of Gorky's most famous poems. In this poem, he symbolizes revolution with storms, and the petrel with revolutionary poets—it can also be said to be himself. Translator's note. Above the misty sea surface,

Dense clouds are whipped by the wind,

Between the dark clouds and the waves,

The petrel proudly sweeps past,

Like a dark flash of lightning.

·····················

For a while, its wings touch the waves,

For a while, it flies close to the dark clouds,

It cries out sharply,

In the midst of this jubilant and urgent storm;

Its cries report to the dark clouds…

Angry force, passionate flames,

The joy of future victory!

····················

Seagulls moan in the face of the storm,

Hurrying and scurrying,

Afraid of being buried in the unfathomable seabed.

Diving birds sigh,

Why sigh,

Because they don't feel the engaging joy of war,

And the rumbling thunder frightens them.

··················

Foolish penguins, timidly

Hide their bellies in caves.

Only the petrel is,

Independently, boldly,

Flying alone over the surging waves.

···················

The lowering dark clouds get darker and get closer,

The waves are eager to meet the thunderbolt.

Look! The thunderbolt rings out… boom,

The wind and waves rise up.

Look! The wind tightly embraces the waves,

Forcefully laying them horizontally on the edge of the rocks,

Taking advantage of a burst of fierce anger

Smashing the huge waves—emerald blocks—

Into foam and droplets.

·····················

Look! The petrel flies like it's sweeping,

Like a dark flash of lightning…

It shoots through the dark clouds like an arrow,

It uses its wings to cut the waves into pieces.

·····················

Proud, dark, herald of the storm,

It mocks the thunderbolt's raging fury.

It is the wise and discerning demon…

In the rumbling thunder,

It has long seen and felt,

The signal of timid surrender…

It is confident in the victory of the sun's light and heat,

Above the dark masses.

······················

Whistling wind, rumbling thunder,

Like deep blue blazing fireworks!

Dark clouds cover the waves,

The ocean captures the light of lightning,

Extinguishing it in its chest,

Its reflection flashes for a while,

For a while, it disappears into the salty water like a fiery snake.

······················

Look? The storm is coming, the storm is coming!

On the turbulent sea, in the midst of lightning,

The petrel sweeps past triumphantly.

It pre-sings the song of victory in a sharp voice…

Hail the great coming storm!

Supplement to the Local News of Shen Bao

Talk

Peiping Universities Get Rebuked

— Wu

A Central News Agency dispatch from January 28th contains news about Peiping universities, which roughly says that our Ministry of Education believes that the various actions of Peiping universities, such as escaping exams and taking early vacations due to the tightening of the situation in Yuguan, are quite inappropriate. "It is found that university students are the backbone of the nation, how can they be allowed to be alarmed and ruin school rules, and 'the school authorities have not reported, which is close to condoning, and is also inappropriate,'" so it telegraphed to all Peiping universities, "The schools should quickly report the situation of students escaping exams and taking early vacations in detail for verification and handling, and report the date of the start of classes for the next semester as well."

Once this order was issued in the capital, needless to say, the schools, which were "also inappropriate," naturally had to submit a report in compliance with the order, needless to say. However, judging from this, the uselessness of Peiping university students, after being "verified and confirmed" by the central government, is indeed undeniably confirmed.

The government takes the blood and sweat of many common people to run universities, originally to cultivate "backbone elements" as "talents" to govern the country and bring peace to the world. Now, when this "national crisis is at hand," they not only cannot defend their "own" country and defend the homeland, but even just with the warning of the tightening of the situation in Yuguan, they "ruin school rules" and flee in a puff of smoke. Isn't this too ungrateful to the national education? Moreover, even if we take a hundred steps back, even if Japanese imperialism immediately attacked Peiping, it would not be too late to abandon their seals and flee with the officials defending the land at that time. Although they might not be able to win the patriotic fame of "perishing with the city," at least they would not lose the responsibility of "backbone elements," right? Moreover, Peiping is still a dignified "cultural city," how can it be asserted that the Japanese imperial soldiers will destroy the "treasure of Oriental culture" in the same way that cannon destroyed the Oriental Library? If that were the case, then running to the East Legation Quarter, living in a high place, what can they do to me? In fact, when Peiping is also incorporated into the territory of a puppet state, isn't there a way to get promoted and become wealthy? So Peiping university students are really too unable to see the big picture and too useless.

However, Peiping university students are not completely useless. For example, the "May Fourth" Movement and the "March 18th" Massacre are all glorious historical records. It's just that "teaching children to become lepers, one generation is not as good as the next."

As for the "school authorities" being rebuked as "also inappropriate," it is even more deserved. Who told them to "have not reported so far"? Isn't this close to condoning? If they had submitted a report in accordance with the regulations afterward, wouldn't the procedures be complete and without any responsibility? Could it be that after demanding salary and striking, they didn't even have time to write a report? So well deserved, well deserved, a third well deserved.

However, now is not the time to "bury oneself in books" or "follow the old ways." What is needed now is to recognize the great enemy in front of us, to sacrifice for the future of the nation. In particular, enlightened university students should join the vast ranks to sweep away the obstacles to national revolution and seize a bright future. So, it is not such a big deal that students temporarily abandon their studies for the sake of fighting for the nation.

Science

Tung Oil Prosperity

— Zhanneng

"Tung oil" is a very important coating, very suitable for decorating houses. Applying it to wooden or ironware can prevent wood from rotting and iron from rusting. It can also be used as a raw material for white porcelain glaze, floor oil, and various other daily necessities. Therefore, I think it is of great research value. I will now briefly describe its properties, manufacturing, uses, and inspection methods below.

(1) Properties | The film formed by raw tung oil lacks elasticity and is uneven. Therefore, only cooked tung oil that has been boiled can be used. The characteristic of tung oil is that it can solidify at 500 degrees Fahrenheit or higher and is insoluble in thinners. However, if mixed with other types of oil, its solidification point will often decrease.

(2) Manufacturing | There are many methods for manufacturing tung oil. I will now introduce the methods used in China, the United States, and Germany below.

(A) Chinese manufacturing method ·· Add two qian each of litharge and massicot to ten jin of tung oil, put it in a pot and boil it, stirring constantly with a wooden stick. When it has boiled four or five times, pour it into an earthenware bowl and stir it constantly until it has cooled completely. (The heat should be moderate, neither too strong nor too weak, to prevent the tung oil from becoming too old or too raw. The added litharge and massicot are only for easy drying and gloss, and have no other effect.)

(B) American manufacturing method ·· Take ten gallons of tung oil and place it in a copper pot, heat it slowly to 350 degrees Fahrenheit, then add ten pounds of lead-manganese soap. After it has completely dissolved, add five gallons of pure linseed oil, stirring constantly. When the temperature reaches 400 degrees Fahrenheit, maintain it for half an hour, then remove from the heat and add two to three gallons of thinner to obtain the desired product.

(C) German manufacturing method; Heat the oil to 216 degrees Celsius, maintain it for one hour, stirring constantly, without stopping. After removing from the heat, it can be thinned with turpentine.

(3) Uses | Tung oil has a wide range of uses, which are briefly described below.

(A) Porcelain glaze: Grind tung oil, rosin, artificial varnish, and translucent porcelain together to obtain a white porcelain glaze, suitable for decorating houses. If the oil is heavy and the resin is light, it can be applied to woodenware.

(B) Protective film oil ·· A mixed oil made of a small amount of tung oil and a large amount of stearin is called protective film oil. When applied to three-in-one soil, it can fill the micro-gaps. At the same time, the tung oil in it will vaporize to form a solid protective film to protect the three-in-one soil so that it will not have chips flying after being trampled.

(C) Waterproof oil: Tung oil and glue can be used to make waterproof oil. When applied to machinery and pipe joints in water, it can prevent water erosion.

(D) Wall paint: Made from tung oil and rosin, when applied to walls, it can be washed with water or exposed to rain.

(E) Floor oil: Mix a little stearin into tung oil to make floor oil. It leaves no marks when stepped on and does not come off when washed with water. It is most suitable for use in trains and ships.

(F) Brushing oil: Also known as baking oil, it is used for painting car canopies and heaters. It can last for a long time. It is made by boiling tung oil, soybean oil, and a small amount of stearin to 520 degrees Fahrenheit.

(4) Inspection | To inspect the superiority of tung oil, if it is heated to 540 degrees, the pure oil will solidify into a light-colored solid. When cut with a knife, it will not be sticky. If the color of the oil is darker and sticky, it is evidence of adulteration.

Yangchun Noodles

— Qileng

Because I always wake up late every day and don't have time to eat breakfast, I always eat Yangchun noodles.

It was a Friday afternoon, and Lao Chen sat in the dormitory listlessly, as if he had something on his mind.

"Lao Chen! Why are you so unhappy today?" Lao Zhang asked him.

"I've run out of money for this week. I have two hao left for the fare home. I'm worried that I'll have to starve tomorrow morning," Lao Chen said with a sad face, at a loss.

"Fool! Are you afraid of not having money to eat Yangchun noodles? The living must find a way to live," Lao Zhang said with a mischievous look.

"Do you have a good idea? Please tell me, I'm willing to follow your good advice."

"To be honest, if you act according to the law, you won't have to worry about not having food," Lao Zhang said as if he had a plan in mind. Originally, Lao Zhang had the nickname Zhu Zhishan, and now I don't know what trick he has come up with again.

"Stop beating around the bush," Lao Chen urged.

So Lao Zhang whispered a few words into Lao Chen's ear.

"Wonderful plan! Wonderful plan!" Lao Chen jumped up happily.

···················

After dinner, Lao Fan knocked on his bowl and came into the room.

"Hey! Lao Fan! Miss Li sent a letter, do you want it?" Lao Chen opened the conversation first.

"Where is it?"

"It's here," Lao Zhang opened the drawer and took out a very large envelope.

"But I can give it to you, but you have to agree to conditions," Lao Chen winked at Lao Zhang.

"Lao Chen! You want to rip me off? That won't work, I'd rather not have the letter," Lao Fan had already seen through their tricks and pretended to be calm.

"It's an express letter, Lao Fan! Look at all the stamps on it. And it's so thick, maybe there's a handkerchief or a photo inside," Lao Zhang shook the letter in his hand a few times.

"Oh! Today is Friday, maybe she's asking you to see a movie tomorrow. I think you should agree to our conditions immediately; can an express letter be delayed for even a minute? My conditions are also very cheap, two bowls of Yangchun noodles, only 240 wen will do," Lao Chen said seriously.

"Okay, I agree to your conditions, you can give me the letter," Lao Fan finally fell into their trap.

"Wait, you must know that fair trade, old and young alike, is not deceived, and all relatives and friends are not in debt," Lao Zhang said a lot.

Lao Fan gave in and first gave them twenty-four copper coins, and then they gave him the letter.

"No, you've already stolen the letter paper," a minute later, Lao Fan opened the letter and saw that it was a ball of waste paper inside, and shouted.

"Let me tell you," Lao Chen said ·· "Originally, we didn't have money to eat Yangchun noodles tomorrow morning. This is the wonderful method that Lao Zhang came up with. He stole the envelope from Miss Li's previous letter, stuffed a ball of waste paper inside, sealed it, and pretended to come and deceive you. Please look at the date on it."

"Haha!" Zhang Zhang couldn't help laughing.

Lao Fan, seeing that he had fallen for their trick, was so angry that he didn't say a word.

To Love Is to Love the Country

— Xiaoheng

The Minimum Standard of Patriotism

Isn't patriotism the most fashionable slogan in society today? Aren't patriotic men the people that everyone admires and respects today?

It's a bit shameful to say! I've been mixing in society for half my life, maybe more than half my life. I often ask myself: Have I ever done one or two patriotic things? But my conscience's answer is a very simple two words: None. But I have also reflected on myself, can all my past behaviors be considered unpatriotic? My self-confidence also resolutely answers me with two words: No.

Speaking of this, my opinion needs to be explained in detail. Because I have not done any patriotic undertakings, of course I cannot be considered patriotic. This is a very obvious principle, and there is no need to talk about it. As for the reason why I dare to be confident that I am not unpatriotic, it is because in
